
Processing AGDRP and NZ DRP claims in Process Direct 003-21111107

-   Background
-   Process
-   References
-   Resources
-   Training & Support

[Expand/Collapse all sections]Expand all

This is a Family and Domestic Violence Interaction Point. If the
customer is with another person, on speaker phone, or already identified
with family and domestic violence concerns, continue with the current
business conversation. Otherwise, go to the Family and domestic violence
procedure to conduct the risk identification and referral process.

For the New South Wales Floods – July 2022, AGDRP and NZ DRP claims
cannot be rejected if a customer has claimed for a non-declared Local
Government Area (LGA) in New South Wales and meets all other eligibility
criteria. All other AGDRP and NZ DRP claims that do not meet the
eligibility criteria can be rejected. See the Process page.

For the New South Wales Floods - February 2022, 3 new Local Government
Areas (LGAs), Lake Macquarie, Strathfield and Waverley, were declared on
27 June 2022. Any claims previously rejected for these LGAs – customers
must lodge a new claim. Customers do not need to request an explanation
of the initial decision and these claims must not be re-indexed.

New impact reasons have been added to the online claim. Check the impact
reason selected by the customer. See Impact reasons to decide if the
customer meets the adversely affected criteria.

Reminder: more than one Flexible Support Payment (including AGDRP, NZ
DRP and the Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment) cannot be paid on the same
day.

This page has information to help staff process claims for AGDRP and NZ
DRP in Process Direct where the online claiming channel has been
activated.

Service Officers must not select an activity in Customer First when
Operational Blueprint advises claims are to be processed in Process
Direct.

Always assess a customer's eligibility for payment by also referring to
Eligibility for AGDRP and NZ DRP.

On this page:

Review claim

Process claim

Assess and finalise claim

Customers without a confirmed identity status - ACC or paper claims only

Requesting evidence

Claiming for children and secondary claimants after original claim
granted

Reporting potential fraud

!FFAP screen - processing claims

Customer has been paid the incorrect payment

AGDRP or NZ DRP was incorrectly paid

Deceased or missing family member claims

Review claim

|                                   | Check the New Zealand residence   |
|                                   | status:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Grandfathered (GRF) is a      |
|                                   |     protected Special Category    |
|                                   |     Visa (SCV) holder. AGDRP is   |
|                                   |     the appropriate payment, as   |
|                                   |     the customer is an Australian |
|                                   |     resident                      |
|                                   | -   Transitional (TRA) is a       |
|                                   |     protected SCV holder. AGDRP   |
|                                   |     is the appropriate payment,   |
|                                   |     as the customer is an         |
|                                   |     Australian resident           |
|                                   | -   Not Entitled (NOT) is a       |
|                                   |     non-protected SCV holder. NZ  |
|                                   |     DRP is the appropriate        |
|                                   |     payment                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if Real Time Analysis have  |
|                                   | assessed a claim as ‘not          |
|                                   | eligible’, staff must not do      |
|                                   | further checks or request         |
|                                   | evidence from the customer. This  |
|                                   | will show in the DOA DOC and      |

|                                   | screen under the Document         |
|                                   | list/note section. Staff can      |
|                                   | reject these claims if approval   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is there information recorded in  |

| 4                                 | Review Keywords + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Keywords may be added to a claim  |
|                                   | to indicate:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Some AGDRP claims are excluded    |
|                                   | from automation (straight through |
|                                   | processing), where they do not    |
|                                   | meet the strict business rules to |
|                                   | enable the system to determine a  |
|                                   | grant outcome and need a manual   |
|                                   | assessment to be completed to     |
|                                   | make sure the accuracy of the     |
|                                   | outcome. The most common          |
|                                   | exclusion reasons will show on    |
|                                   | the Keywords page to help staff   |
|                                   | in processing claims. See         |
|                                   | Resources for the list of         |
|                                   | exclusion keywords and reasons    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If a claim is excluded from   |
|                                   |     automation, the customer may  |
|                                   |     still be eligible for         |
|                                   |     payment. If an exclusion      |
|                                   |     keyword shows, this may not   |
|                                   |     be the only reason the claim  |
|                                   |     was excluded from automation  |
|                                   | -   Not all exclusion keywords    |
|                                   |     are listed on the Resources   |
|                                   |     page                          |
|                                   | -   Service Officers must follow  |
|                                   |     all process steps in this     |
|                                   |     Operational Blueprint to      |
|                                   |     review the claim fully        |
|                                   |     including any exclusion       |
|                                   |     reason, to determine if a     |
|                                   |     customer is eligible or       |
|                                   |     ineligible for the payment    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The claim should be allocated to  |
|                                   | appropriately trained staff for   |
|                                   | processing. These will have a     |
|                                   | keyword attached. For example,    |
|                                   | NOM is for claims with a payment  |
|                                   | nominee where the X032AS - No     |
|                                   | Payment Destination, please       |
|                                   | update via PA screen error shows  |
|                                   | in Process Direct, FAOCHI is for  |
|                                   | claims where a shared care        |
|                                   | assessment or addition of a new   |
|                                   | child is needed. If a claim has   |
|                                   | been assigned incorrectly to a    |
|                                   | Service Officer without the       |
|                                   | necessary training:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the Inbox in Process    |
|                                   |     Direct:                       |
|                                   |     - In Main Category select WLM |
|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   |     - Select Multi-Select         |
|                                   |     - Select the transaction from |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   |     - Select Unassign at the      |
|                                   |     bottom of the screen to       |
|                                   |     unassign the claim with       |
|                                   |     Reason of Second contact      |
|                                   |     attempt required              |
|                                   |     - Select Submit               |
|                                   | -   The claim will then be        |
|                                   |     reallocated to an             |
|                                   |     appropriately trained Service |
|                                   |     Officer to make the           |
|                                   |     assessment                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Action needed for the claim       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See Resources for a list of   |
|                                   |     keywords used in Process      |
|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   | -   Select the Keywords icon      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claim is under review by a        |
|                                   | specialist fraud team. If the     |
|                                   | keyword:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   FRDCHK is listed, staff must  |
|                                   |     not action the claim          |
|                                   |     - In Main Category select WLM |
|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   |     - Select Multi-Select         |
|                                   |     - Select the transaction from |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   |     - Select Unassign at the      |
|                                   |     bottom of the screen to       |
|                                   |     unassign the claim with       |
|                                   |     Reason of Recategorised       |
|                                   |     - Note: if the option         |
|                                   |     Recategorised does not work,  |
|                                   |     select User unavailable       |
|                                   |     - Select Submit               |
|                                   |     - The claim will then be      |
|                                   |     allocated to an appropriately |
|                                   |     trained Service Officer to    |
|                                   |     make the assessment           |
|                                   |     - Procedure ends here         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claim has been reviewed by a      |
|                                   | specialist fraud team and is      |
|                                   | cleared to process. If the        |
|                                   | keyword:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   FRDASS is listed, the claim   |
|                                   |     has been cleared of integrity |
|                                   |     risks and qualification       |
|                                   |     should be assessed as normal  |
|                                   | -   FRDREJ is listed, reject the  |
|                                   |     claim, if approval has:       |
|                                   |     - been given to reject        |
|                                   |     claims, process the claim.    |
|                                   |     Note: no customer contact is  |
|                                   |     needed. See Table 2           |
|                                   |     - not been given, follow      |
|                                   |     Table 3 Step 2 to place the   |
|                                   |     claim on hold                 |
|                                   | -   If the keywords FRDCHK or     |
|                                   |     FRDREJ are not listed, go to  |
|                                   |     Step 5                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For the                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | New South Wales Floods - July     |
|                                   | 2022 claims with any of the       |
|                                   | following keywords STP262,        |
|                                   | STP272, STP276, STP277, STP323,   |
|                                   | STP341 must be reviewed by the    |
|                                   | Service Officer to determine      |
|                                   | eligibility. They must not be     |

|                                   |     ineligible)                   |

| 5                                 | Claim status + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The claim status must be In       |
|                                   | Process before it can be          |
|                                   | processed.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a status of Submission   |
|                                   | Failed shows, this is due to an   |
|                                   | error between the claim           |
|                                   | submission and claim activity     |
|                                   | generating. This can happen due   |
|                                   | to conflicting activities on the  |
|                                   | customer or partner record, or    |
|                                   | record locking when the claim is  |
|                                   | submitted. To action these, see   |
|                                   | Step 6 in the Overview of the     |
|                                   | family assistance and/or PPL      |
|                                   | online claim process table. For   |
|                                   | help, contact Technical Peer      |
|                                   | Support.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the claim status In Process?   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, go to Step 6                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, for claim status definitions  |
|                                   | and action to take, see Process   |
|                                   | Direct navigation, common screens |
|                                   | and functions                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Hold reasons: consider        |
|                                   |     whether to return the claim   |
|                                   |     to In Process. For example,   |
|                                   |     evidence/POI has been         |
|                                   |     provided, customer now lives  |
|                                   |     in the expanded area, system  |
|                                   |     issue resolved. Go to Step 6  |
|                                   | -   To reassess a previously      |
|                                   |     rejected claim:               |
|                                   |     - If rejected FSD, FRC or     |
|                                   |     POI, see Requested            |
|                                   |     documentation not provided    |
|                                   |     resulting in rejection of new |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   | -   To reassess an incorrectly    |
|                                   |     rejected claim:               |
|                                   |     - To re-index the claim,      |
|                                   |     refer to directions for SAP   |
|                                   |     online claims in Cancelling   |
|                                   |     claim activities and          |
|                                   |     re-indexing claims            |

| 6                                 | Review claim details and check    |
|                                   | for previous claim + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: For the New South Wales     |
|                                   | Floods – February 2022, 3 new     |
|                                   | Local Government Areas (LGAs),    |
|                                   | Lake Macquarie, Strathfield and   |
|                                   | Waverley, were declared on 27     |
|                                   | June 2022. Any claims previously  |
|                                   | rejected for these LGAs –         |
|                                   | customers must lodge a new claim. |
|                                   | Customers do not need to request  |
|                                   | an explanation of the initial     |
|                                   | decision and these claims must    |
|                                   | not be re-indexed.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the information provided   |
|                                   | by the customer.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select [Open left slider; Close   |
|                                   | right slider] and [Enter full     |
|                                   | screen] to view the Claim Summary |
|                                   | in a new window. If it is blank,  |
|                                   | press [F5] to refresh the page.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Continually reference information |
|                                   | within the Claim Summary when     |
|                                   | processing a customer’s claim, as |
|                                   | not all information is recorded   |
|                                   | on the system.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer has claimed the     |
|                                   | incorrect event or payment        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Assess the claim as per the       |
|                                   | details in the Claim Summary      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must cancel the claim and   |
|                                   | change the event to align with    |
|                                   | the event and payment the         |
|                                   | customer should have applied for. |
|                                   | How to do this will be outlined   |
|                                   | later                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note down the Claim ID            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If possible, keep the Claim   |
|                                   |     Summary open                  |
|                                   | -   This will make it easier to   |
|                                   |     access the customer’s         |
|                                   |     original claim details to     |
|                                   |     enter into the new claim      |
|                                   |     without having to search for  |
|                                   |     the initial Claim ID          |
|                                   | -   If the Claim Summary closes,  |
|                                   |     it can be accessed by         |
|                                   |     returning to the Inbox icon   |
|                                   |     on the Process Direct landing |
|                                   |     page, and entering the Claim  |
|                                   |     ID into the Claim Id: field   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer meets all         |
|                                   | eligibility criteria for the      |
|                                   | event and payment they should     |
|                                   | have applied for their claim can  |
|                                   | be granted                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer should have   |
|                                   | claimed:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | NZ DRP instead of AGDRP           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Customer contact will be      |
|                                   |     needed to request evidence of |
|                                   |     the NZ DRP customer’s         |
|                                   |     participation in the          |
|                                   |     Australian taxation system.   |
|                                   |     These claims cannot be        |
|                                   |     granted until this evidence   |
|                                   |     is provided                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | AGDRP but claimed NZ DRP, if the  |
|                                   | customer claimed for a            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   dependent adult, spouse or    |
|                                   |     child who lives with them     |
|                                   |     (who is not their dependent   |
|                                   |     child), these must not to be  |
|                                   |     included in the customer’s    |
|                                   |     AGDRP claim                   |
|                                   |     - No customer contact is      |
|                                   |     needed                        |
|                                   |     - The customer will receive a |
|                                   |     decision letter               |
|                                   |     - If they disagree, they can  |
|                                   |     request a review of the       |
|                                   |     decision                      |
|                                   | -   dependent child/ren, include  |
|                                   |     them in the customers AGDRP   |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For claims lodged:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   on or after 11 March 2022,    |
|                                   |     new impact reasons have been  |
|                                   |     added to the online claim and |
|                                   |     ACC for customers to select.  |
|                                   |     See Impact reasons to         |
|                                   |     determine if the impact       |
|                                   |     reason the customer has       |
|                                   |     selected and any free text    |
|                                   |     information provided, meets   |
|                                   |     the adversely affected        |
|                                   |     criteria                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer:              |
|                                   | - has selected a valid (eligible) |
|                                   | impact reason and completed the   |
|                                   | free text field, customer contact |
|                                   | is needed if the free text        |
|                                   | information does not support the  |
|                                   | impact reason selected. For       |
|                                   | example, a customer may have      |
|                                   | selected ‘The interior of my home |
|                                   | has been exposed to the           |
|                                   | elements’, however the free text  |
|                                   | field has that rainwater came     |
|                                   | through a gap in a closed window. |
|                                   | Rainwater entering through a gap  |
|                                   | in a door or window that is       |
|                                   | closed or open does not meet the  |
|                                   | eligibility criteria. See         |
|                                   | Eligibility for AGDRP and NZ DRP. |
|                                   | Do not contact the customer yet.  |
|                                   | Review all eligibility criteria   |
|                                   | first                             |
|                                   | - meets all other eligibility     |
|                                   | criteria, their claim can be      |
|                                   | granted with no further customer  |
|                                   | contact. If an invalid            |
|                                   | (ineligible) impact reason is     |
|                                   | selected, however free text       |
|                                   | information supports a valid      |
|                                   | impact reason. For example, a     |
|                                   | customer may have selected        |
|                                   | ‘Clothing, toys, bicycles or      |
|                                   | gardens were damaged or           |
|                                   | destroyed’ however free text      |
|                                   | information has ‘flood waters     |
|                                   | came in, damaging the inside of   |
|                                   | my home, including clothing and   |
|                                   | toys’                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   on or before 10 March 2022,   |
|                                   |     compare any information       |
|                                   |     provided in free text fields  |
|                                   |     with the Impact reasons to    |
|                                   |     determine if the customer     |
|                                   |     meets the adversely affected  |
|                                   |     criteria                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | does not meet any of the          |
|                                   | adversely affected criteria, they |
|                                   | do not meet the eligibility       |
|                                   | criteria for AGDRP or NZ DRP. The |
|                                   | claim should be rejected. If      |
|                                   | approval has:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   been given to reject claims,  |
|                                   |     process the claim. See Table  |
|                                   |     2                             |
|                                   | -   not been given, see Step 2 in |
|                                   |     Table 3 to place the claim on |
|                                   |     hold                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | meets at least one of the         |
|                                   | adversely affected criteria, or   |
|                                   | customer contact is needed to     |
|                                   | discuss free text information,    |
|                                   | continue assessing their claim    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For paper claims:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select [Quick link] from the  |
|                                   |     bottom of the open Process    |
|                                   |     Direct window, or             |
|                                   | -   select Documents from the     |
|                                   |     icon menu                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To assess the customer’s          |
|                                   | eligibility when reviewing claim  |
|                                   | details, see Eligibility for      |
|                                   | AGDRP and NZ DRP.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If at any time when processing    |
|                                   | the claim, the staff member       |
|                                   | suspects fraudulent claims from   |
|                                   | the customer in relation to their |
|                                   | identity or circumstances, go to  |
|                                   | Step 22.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has claimed for   |
|                                   | the incorrect event or payment,   |
|                                   | go to Step 7.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Otherwise, go to Step 8.          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Customer has claimed the          |
|                                   | incorrect event or payment + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer’s claim will need to |
|                                   | be cancelled and the correct      |
|                                   | event and/or payment selected.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Notes icon             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note on the DL screen under the   |
|                                   | Document list/note section to     |
|                                   | indicate why the claim is being   |
|                                   | cancelled                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   For example:                  |
|                                   |     - the customer should have    |
|                                   |     claimed AGDRP but claimed NZ  |
|                                   |     DRP. Claim ID is being        |
|                                   |     cancelled and new claim       |
|                                   |     created for the correct       |
|                                   |     payment type (AGDRP)          |
|                                   |     - the customer has claimed    |
|                                   |     for the New South Wales       |
|                                   |     Floods, February 2022 but     |
|                                   |     their address at the time of  |
|                                   |     the event shows they should   |
|                                   |     have claimed for the South    |
|                                   |     East Queensland Floods,       |
|                                   |     February 2022. Claim ID is    |
|                                   |     being cancelled and new claim |
|                                   |     created under the correct     |
|                                   |     event (South East Queensland  |
|                                   |     Floods, February 2022)        |
|                                   | -   If relevant, also include in  |
|                                   |     the Progress of Claim Note on |
|                                   |     the DL screen under the       |
|                                   |     Document list/note section    |
|                                   |     where a customer should have  |
|                                   |     claimed AGDRP instead of NZ   |
|                                   |     DRP and was not eligible to   |
|                                   |     claim for a dependent adult,  |
|                                   |     spouse or child who lives     |
|                                   |     with them (who is not their   |
|                                   |     dependent child)              |
|                                   |     - Select Save                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close document       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Status icon            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Change status (pencil) |
|                                   | icon                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Not Effective from the     |
|                                   | drop down                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Save                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note down the Customer’s CRN      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will go back to the  |
|                                   | Process Direct Landing Page       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Scroll down to the bottom of the  |
|                                   | screen and select the SOA Shell   |
|                                   | tile                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Benefit type field from    |
|                                   | the drop down for:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   AGDRP select Disaster         |
|                                   |     Recovery Payment              |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP select New Zealand     |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment - Ex-gratia  |
|                                   | -   Never select Emergency        |
|                                   |     payments                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Customer CRN field, enter  |
|                                   | the customer’s CRN                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Date of receipt field,     |
|                                   | enter the Claim submission date   |
|                                   | in the Claim Summary              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Create claim in the bottom |
|                                   | right hand corner                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Process at the bottom      |
|                                   | right of the claim to start       |
|                                   | entering claim details as per the |
|                                   | original Claim Summary            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Although all relevant Task        |
|                                   | Selectors will be automatically   |
|                                   | selected, staff only need to      |
|                                   | complete the Disaster Recovery    |
|                                   | Task Selector at this point to    |
|                                   | enter all relevant claim details  |
|                                   | from the customer’s original      |
|                                   | claim                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   All other Task Selectors will |
|                                   |     be checked later in Table 2   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Disaster event – staff must       |
|                                   | carefully select the correct      |
|                                   | event and/or payment the customer |
|                                   | should have claimed for in their  |
|                                   | original claim                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Due to the number of events   |
|                                   |     that can be selected in the   |
|                                   |     drop down (especially for NZ  |
|                                   |     DRP) type in the correct      |
|                                   |     event code to select the      |
|                                   |     event                         |
|                                   | -   To find the correct event     |
|                                   |     code, see Keywords for this   |
|                                   |     event (codes) in the          |
|                                   |     Resources page of the         |
|                                   |     Operational Blueprint for the |
|                                   |     event                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue           |

|                                   | Complete all Eligibility          |
|                                   | questions as per the original     |
|                                   | Claim Summary                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | during the event as per the       |

|                                   |     child(ren)                    |

|                                   | Complete the Living in Australian |
|                                   | questions as per the original     |
|                                   | Claim Summary                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete the Assessment of damage |
|                                   | and/or destruction as per the     |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter the detail of any Injured   |

|                                   | original Claim Summary            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter any Dependent child(ren)    |
|                                   | impact details as per the         |
|                                   | original Claim Summary            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | select Next to continue           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not finalise (reject or grant) |
|                                   | the claim yet                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Continue assessing and processing |
|                                   | the claim                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 8                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Claiming for a concurrent event + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claims must be checked where a    |
|                                   | customer is trying to claim for a |
|                                   | concurrent event. This is where a |
|                                   | customer has been paid for the:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   New South Wales Floods –      |
|                                   |     February 2022 and now         |
|                                   |     claiming the South East       |
|                                   |     Queensland Floods – February  |
|                                   |     2022, or                      |
|                                   | -   South East Queensland Floods  |
|                                   |     – February 2022 and now       |
|                                   |     claiming the New South Wales  |
|                                   |     Floods – February 2022        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Keywords icon to   |
|                                   |     see if STP352 Customer        |
|                                   |     already granted for           |
|                                   |     concurrent event shows        |
|                                   | -   Select the Notes icon         |
|                                   | -   Scroll down and select >      |
|                                   |     Notes                         |
|                                   | -   In the Content column, check  |
|                                   |     for a note that shows the     |
|                                   |     customer has been granted for |
|                                   |     the New South Wales Floods -  |
|                                   |     February 2022 or South East   |
|                                   |     Queensland Floods - February  |
|                                   |     2022                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the keyword or Notes show    |
|                                   | the customer has been granted and |
|                                   | paid for the New South Wales      |
|                                   | Floods - February 2022 or the     |
|                                   | South East Queensland Floods -    |
|                                   | February 2022 and the customer is |
|                                   | now trying to claim for a         |
|                                   | concurrent event?                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 9             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 10             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Customer has claimed for a        |
|                                   | concurrent event                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer’s claim for the   |
|                                   | concurrent event does not meet    |
|                                   | all eligibility criteria + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If approval has:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   been given to reject claims,  |
|                                   |     process the claim. See Table  |
|                                   |     2                             |
|                                   | -   not been given, see Step 2 in |
|                                   |     Table 3 to place the claim on |
|                                   |     hold                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer’s claim for the   |
|                                   | concurrent event does meet all    |
|                                   | eligibility criteria and they may |
|                                   | be eligible for both events +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Copy the Claim ID for the granted |
|                                   | claim                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Click on Inbox                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter the Claim ID for the        |
|                                   | granted claim into the Claim Id:  |
|                                   | field                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the claim summary,         |
|                                   | including address details         |
|                                   | provided by the customer in their |
|                                   | claim                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the Address history by     |
|                                   | keying 'ADH' next to Super Key    |
|                                   | and press [Enter]                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are any address changes  |
|                                   | after 1 January 2022, review the  |
|                                   | date the agency was notified by   |
|                                   | the customer by keying ‘DL’ next  |
|                                   | to Super Key and press [Enter],   |
|                                   | then reviewing any CUS COA UPD    |
|                                   | CLI AAC Update Finalisation Note  |
|                                   | or DOCs                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Note: if no Note or DOC       |
|                                   |     appears, key ‘HAL’ next to    |
|                                   |     Super Key and press [Enter]   |
|                                   |     to go to the Historical       |
|                                   |     Activity List (HAL) screen    |
|                                   |     and check when the activity   |
|                                   |     ID for the address update was |
|                                   |     coded (the activity ID can be |
|                                   |     taken from ADH screen)        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer was granted       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   for damage to a principal     |
|                                   |     place of residence and is     |
|                                   |     claiming a concurrent event   |
|                                   |     due to an injury immediate    |
|                                   |     family member who is deceased |
|                                   |     or missing, contact Technical |
|                                   |     Peer Support, who must        |
|                                   |     - escalate the claim to the   |
|                                   |     Level 2 Helpdesk using the    |
|                                   |     payment query template        |
|                                   |     - place the claim on hold     |
|                                   |     with the reason Awaiting      |
|                                   |     policy advice                 |
|                                   |     - the Level 2 Helpdesk will   |
|                                   |     determine next steps          |
|                                   |     - do not process the          |
|                                   |     customer’s claim              |
|                                   |     - procedure ends here         |
|                                   | -   due to an injury or immediate |
|                                   |     family member who is deceased |
|                                   |     or missing and is claiming a  |
|                                   |     concurrent event due to       |
|                                   |     damage to a principal place   |
|                                   |     of residence, contact         |
|                                   |     Technical Peer Support who    |
|                                   |     must                          |
|                                   |     -escalate the claim to the    |
|                                   |     Level 2 Helpdesk using the    |
|                                   |     payment query template        |
|                                   |     -place the claim on hold with |
|                                   |     the reason Awaiting policy    |
|                                   |     advice                        |
|                                   |     - the Level 2 Helpdesk will   |
|                                   |     determine next steps          |
|                                   |     - do not process the          |
|                                   |     customer’s claim              |
|                                   |     - procedure ends here         |
|                                   | -   for a major damage impact     |
|                                   |     reason, the concurrent claim  |
|                                   |     is for another major damage   |
|                                   |     impact reason and the         |
|                                   |     customer changed their        |
|                                   |     address on or after each      |
|                                   |     event start date (for event   |
|                                   |     start dates, see the          |
|                                   |     Operational Blueprint for the |
|                                   |     event) either by way of the   |
|                                   |     Claim Summary or as detailed  |
|                                   |     in a CUS COA UPD CLI AAC      |
|                                   |     Update Finalisation Note,     |
|                                   |     -attempt to contact the       |
|                                   |     customer to request evidence  |
|                                   |     for the address change, as    |
|                                   |     well as any other evidence    |
|                                   |     needed to support the         |
|                                   |     customer’s claim that has not |
|                                   |     yet been provided. For        |
|                                   |     example, evidence of          |
|                                   |     participation in the          |
|                                   |     Australian tax system for NZ  |
|                                   |     DRP customers                 |
|                                   |     -see Table 5                  |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     - do not process the          |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note on the DL screen under the   |

|                                   | record                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The customer should have      |
|                                   |     claimed for the South East    |

|                                   |     paid for both events          |
|                                   | -   A debt ACTDOC has not been    |
|                                   |     created as it has been        |
|                                   |     determined the customer       |
|                                   |     qualified for AGDRP/NZ DRP    |
|                                   |     for the South East Queensland |
|                                   |     Floods – February 2022        |
|                                   |     instead of the New South      |
|                                   |     Wales Floods – February 2022  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Save                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Close document             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If approval has:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   been given to reject claims,  |
|                                   |     process the claim. See Table  |
|                                   |     2                             |
|                                   | -   not been given, see Step 2 in |
|                                   |     Table 3 to place the claim on |
|                                   |     hold                          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 10                                | Claiming for same event + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer already claimed  |
|                                   | for this event? If no go to Step  |
|                                   | 16.                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If yes, is the customer wanting   |
|                                   | to claim:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | AGDRP/NZ DRP for a dependent      |
|                                   | child/ren they did not include in |
|                                   | their original claim that was     |
|                                   | granted or that they included in  |
|                                   | their claim and were not paid     |
|                                   | for, or                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | NZ-DRP for a secondary claimant   |
|                                   | (partner, child living with them  |
|                                   | who is not their dependent child, |
|                                   | dependent adult) they did not     |
|                                   | include in their original claim   |
|                                   | that was granted or that they     |
|                                   | included in their original claim  |
|                                   | and were not paid for? Note: a    |
|                                   | customer may have called the      |
|                                   | agency to raise this.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Table 6            |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 11             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 11                                | Reclaiming after rejections or    |
|                                   | withdrawals or being paid for the |
|                                   | same event                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reclaiming after being paid for   |
|                                   | the same event + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer has already been    |
|                                   | paid for the same event, they     |
|                                   | cannot receive another payment,   |
|                                   | even if they have a new and valid |
|                                   | impact reason.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To check if a customer has been   |
|                                   | paid for the same event           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Payment Summary (PS)    |
|                                   | screen by keying PS next to Super |
|                                   | Key and press [Enter]             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Display payments for: select FSP  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Number of months in past:         |
|                                   | defaults to 3. If the event has   |
|                                   | been activated for longer than 3  |
|                                   | months, adjust this number to     |
|                                   | capture relevant period           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Execute                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a Flexible Support Payment     |
|                                   | (FSP) payment shows, select [More |
|                                   | info] to view the Payment         |
|                                   | Components. The Benefit Qualifier |
|                                   | Code will show the event code it  |
|                                   | applied to,                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key 'DL' next to Super Key and    |
|                                   | press [Enter] to check the        |
|                                   | customer’s Document List (DL)     |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review any Claim Finalisation     |
|                                   | Note to determine if the customer |
|                                   | has already been granted for the  |
|                                   | same event                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has been paid for |
|                                   | the same event, the customer      |
|                                   | cannot be paid again and their    |
|                                   | claim must be rejected            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If approval has                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   been given to reject claims,  |
|                                   |     process the claim. See Table  |
|                                   |     2                             |
|                                   | -   not been given, see Step 2 in |
|                                   |     Table 3 to place the claim on |
|                                   |     hold                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reclaiming after rejections or    |
|                                   | withdrawals + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers are able to reclaim for |
|                                   | an event if their previous        |
|                                   | claim(s) have been rejected or    |
|                                   | withdrawn.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | How to check withdrawn and        |
|                                   | rejected claims                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Transactions icon      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   This will show any claims     |
|                                   |     withdrawn or not completed    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select All Transactions           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   This will show all completed  |
|                                   |     claims, including claims:     |
|                                   |     - granted and paid, and       |
|                                   |     - rejected                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Take care when assessing the new  |
|                                   | claim to make sure:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | any previous reasons for          |
|                                   | rejection are taken into account  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   this includes concerns about  |
|                                   |     the validity of the claim or  |
|                                   |     the customer’s identity       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the customer has not changed the  |
|                                   | circumstances in the new claim to |
|                                   | be granted a payment              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | claimants are not issued another  |
|                                   | payment for the same event if the |
|                                   | AGDRP or NZ DRP is to be granted  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   this includes children, and   |
|                                   |     secondary claimants (NZ DRP)  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Why has the customer lodged a new |
|                                   | claim for the same event?         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Previous claim(s) was rejected,   |
|                                   | go to Step 12                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Previous claim(s) was withdrawn   |
|                                   | before the claim was processed:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Withdrawn once (one           |
|                                   |     withdrawal and 2 claims       |
|                                   |     lodged), go to Step 16        |
|                                   | -   Withdrawn 2 times or more     |
|                                   |     (minimum of 2 withdrawals and |
|                                   |     3 claim lodgements), go to    |
|                                   |     Step 14                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 12                                | Claim for same event previously   |
|                                   | rejected + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Find the Notes for the rejected   |
|                                   | claim to identify the reason for  |
|                                   | the rejection.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Also, find the previous claim by  |
|                                   | selecting the Transactions icon   |
|                                   | and locating the Claim ID. Select |
|                                   | the hyperlink and review the      |
|                                   | Claim Summary and any             |
|                                   | attachments. Compare the original |
|                                   | details carefully with the new    |
|                                   | claim.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   provided the same information |
|                                   |     about their circumstances,    |
|                                   |     but now meets the criteria,   |
|                                   |     continue to process the       |
|                                   |     claim. For example, a         |
|                                   |     declared area has been        |
|                                   |     expanded, evidence has been   |
|                                   |     provided, go to Step 16       |
|                                   | -   provided the same information |
|                                   |     and still does not meet       |
|                                   |     criteria, the claim is to be  |
|                                   |     rejected go to Table 3 Step 1 |
|                                   |     Note: consider if the         |
|                                   |     customer may be attempting to |
|                                   |     obtain a grant outcome        |
|                                   |     fraudulently. For example,    |
|                                   |     there are repeated claim      |
|                                   |     attempts or withdrawing       |
|                                   |     claims. If, so, go to Step 22 |
|                                   | -   changed their information     |
|                                   |     and/or circumstances from the |
|                                   |     previous claim, go to Step 13 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 13                                | Different circumstances to        |
|                                   | previous rejected claim(s) + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS only) between 8:00 am and    |
|                                   | 8:00 pm using the customer's      |
|                                   | local time, to let them know a    |
|                                   | Service Officer will call them    |
|                                   | today from a private number.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer to clarify   |
|                                   | their situation.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer needs an      |
|                                   | interpreter, the 4 digit office   |

|                                   | interpreter (Interpreter          |
|                                   | Connect).                         |

|                                   |                                   |
