|                                   | give hints or prompts that help   |
|                                   | the customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   | questions                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Tell them they can:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Be provided with an           |
|                                   |     explanation of the reason for |
|                                   |     the rejection. This may also  |
|                                   |     lead to an appeal/review of   |
|                                   |     the original decision         |
|                                   | -   Have the new claim assessed,  |
|                                   |     noting the information in the |
|                                   |     new claim will be compared to |
|                                   |     the previous claim to         |
|                                   |     understand what circumstances |
|                                   |     have changed, and evidence    |
|                                   |     may be requested              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer want an         |
|                                   | explanation of the original       |
|                                   | rejection decision, and           |
|                                   | potentially a review of the       |
|                                   | decision?                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, encourage the customer to    |
|                                   | withdraw their online claim via   |
|                                   | their Centrelink online account   |
|                                   | via myGov whilst on the call.     |
|                                   | Tell the customer their current   |
|                                   | claim must be withdrawn to start  |
|                                   | the explanation and review        |
|                                   | process. Customer to withdraw the |
|                                   | claim via their online account:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Customer withdraws claim      |
|                                   |     while on call                 |
|                                   |     - Follow the process in       |
|                                   |     Request for an explanation or |
|                                   |     application for a formal      |
|                                   |     review                        |
|                                   |     - If the Service Officer has  |
|                                   |     determined evidence is        |
|                                   |     necessary to support a review |
|                                   |     of decision (if requested)    |
|                                   |     and is required before a      |
|                                   |     decision can be made,         |
|                                   |     encourage the customer to     |
|                                   |     upload documents to their     |
|                                   |     record on the day. This will  |
|                                   |     allow their review to be      |
|                                   |     completed as soon as possible |
|                                   |     - Annotate the Progress of    |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document list/note  |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   |     - Select Save                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close document       |
|                                   |     - Procedure ends here         |
|                                   | -   Customer will withdraw claim  |

|                                   |     - Tell the customer the       |
|                                   |     review cannot begin until     |

|                                   |     review cannot start until     |

|                                   |     information discussed         |

|                                   |     - Place the claim On Hold for |
|                                   |     7 days using hold reason      |
|                                   |     Customer to provide           |
|                                   |     information                   |
|                                   |     - Procedure ends here         |
|                                   | -   Service Officer to withdraw   |
|                                   |     claim at request of customer: |
|                                   |     - Follow the process to       |
|                                   |     withdraw a claim in Process   |
|                                   |     Direct, including the         |
|                                   |     required Notes and issuing of |
|                                   |     a Q888 letter. Service        |
|                                   |     Officers should ask TPS for   |
|                                   |     help when needed              |
|                                   |     - Once the claim has been     |
|                                   |     withdrawn, follow the process |
|                                   |     in Request for an explanation |
|                                   |     or application for a formal   |
|                                   |     review                        |
|                                   |     If the Service Officer has    |
|                                   |     determined evidence is        |
|                                   |     necessary to support a review |
|                                   |     of decision (if requested)    |
|                                   |     and this is required before a |
|                                   |     decision can be made,         |
|                                   |     encourage the customer to     |
|                                   |     upload documents to their     |
|                                   |     record on the day. This will  |
|                                   |     allow their review to be      |
|                                   |     completed as soon as possible |
|                                   |     - Annotate the Progress of    |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document list/note  |
|                                   |     section with the outcome of   |
|                                   |     the discussion                |
|                                   |     - Select Save                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close document       |
|                                   |     - Procedure ends here         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, the customer wants their      |
|                                   | pending claim to be assessed.     |

|                                   |     the discussion                |

|                                   |     determined:                   |

|                                   |     - more evidence is necessary  |
|                                   |     to support the change in      |
|                                   |     circumstances, encourage the  |
|                                   |     customer to upload documents  |
|                                   |     via the requested task in the |
|                                   |     online claim to their record  |
|                                   |     on the day. This will allow   |
|                                   |     their claim to be processed   |
|                                   |     as soon as possible           |

|                                   |     2 in Table 5                  |
|                                   |     - If the customer does not    |

| 14                                | Multiple claims and withdrawals   |
|                                   | for same event + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When a customer has withdrawn a   |
|                                   | claim for the same event twice or |
|                                   | more (that is, lodged a claim 3   |
|                                   | times or more), it is reasonable  |
|                                   | to assume the customer is:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   having difficulty completing  |
|                                   |     the online claim (for example |
|                                   |     trying to add extra           |
|                                   |     information to explain their  |
|                                   |     situation, omitted to include |
|                                   |     all children in previous      |
|                                   |     claims)                       |
|                                   | -   trying to avoid having to     |
|                                   |     lodge evidence, if requested  |
|                                   |     on a previous claim, or       |
|                                   | -   may be trying to trigger a    |
|                                   |     ‘grant’ outcome by changing   |
|                                   |     responses                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the claim details in each  |
|                                   | withdrawn claim. To do this,      |
|                                   | click on the Transactions icon    |
|                                   | and select the claim ID (in blue  |
|                                   | text) with a Status of            |
|                                   | ‘Withdrawal confirmed’. Check     |
|                                   | details in the Claim Summary of   |
|                                   | each claim withdrawn for the same |
|                                   | event.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer submitted the    |
|                                   | same information in each claim    |
|                                   | and has not previously been       |
|                                   | requested to provide evidence to  |
|                                   | support their claim?              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, continue with assessment of  |
|                                   | the claim. Go to Step 16          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, and the customer has:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   made minimal changes it is    |
|                                   |     reasonable the customer may   |
|                                   |     have had issues with the      |
|                                   |     claiming process, for         |
|                                   |     example:                      |
|                                   |     -added dependent children not |
|                                   |     previously claimed but linked |
|                                   |     to the customer, or           |
|                                   |     -appears to be attempting to  |
|                                   |     provide further explanation   |
|                                   |     of how impacted               |
|                                   | -   Continue with assessment of   |
|                                   |     the claim. Go to Step 16      |
|                                   | -   changed their responses to    |
|                                   |     the questions in each claim,  |
|                                   |     including their bank account  |
|                                   |     details, go to Step 15        |

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 16                                | Age at date of claim lodgement +  |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the customer’s age at date  |
|                                   | of claim lodgement. If they are   |
|                                   | 18 years of age or older, go to   |
|                                   | Step 18.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is 17 years of    |
|                                   | age or younger, go to Step 17     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 17                                | Age eligibility on any day of     |
|                                   | major disaster + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To be eligible for AGDRP or NZ    |
|                                   | DRP, the customer must be 16      |
|                                   | years of age, or under 16 years   |
|                                   | and receiving an income support   |
|                                   | payment on any day of the event   |
|                                   | period.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The event period (start and end   |
|                                   | date) for each disaster event is  |
|                                   | in the Operational Blueprint for  |
|                                   | the event, Background page >      |
|                                   | Assessing and coding claims.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: to find the Operational     |
|                                   | Blueprint for the event, see      |
|                                   | Current emergency management      |
|                                   | events and select Natural         |
|                                   | Disasters.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For example, for the New South    |
|                                   | Wales Floods - February 2022, the |
|                                   | event commenced on 22 February    |
|                                   | 2022 and ended on 4 May 2022.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The period may range from one day |
|                                   | to several weeks from the date of |
|                                   | activation.                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the impact of a disaster is    |
|                                   | still unfolding, an end date may  |
|                                   | not be published. Staff must      |
|                                   | assess the claim based on         |
|                                   | information available             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer may be 17 at the     |
|                                   | date of claim lodgement but were  |
|                                   | not at least 16 years of age on   |
|                                   | any day of the event period.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the customer at least 16      |
|                                   | years of age, or under 16 years   |
|                                   | and receiving an income support   |
|                                   | payment, on any day of the event  |
|                                   | period?                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, the customer meets the age   |
|                                   | requirement, go to Step 18        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, the claim should be rejected. |
|                                   | If approval has:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   been given to reject claims,  |
|                                   |     process the claim. See Table  |
|                                   |     2                             |
|                                   | -   not been given, see Step 2 in |
|                                   |     Table 3 to place the claim on |
|                                   |     hold                          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 18                                | Tasks + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All evidence for AGDRP and NZ DRP |
|                                   | claims is requested as            |
|                                   | supplementary evidence in an      |
|                                   | online or Assisted Customer       |
|                                   | Claim.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers will be told to         |
|                                   | provide:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Proof of identity (POI) if    |
|                                   |     their Identity Status is Not  |
|                                   |     Confirmed. However, they may  |
|                                   |     still meet the POI            |
|                                   |     requirements for emergency    |
|                                   |     payments                      |
|                                   | -   Evidence of participation in  |
|                                   |     the Australian tax system (NZ |
|                                   |     DRP claimants only). This     |
|                                   |     evidence must be provided     |
|                                   |     before an NZ DRP claim can be |
|                                   |     assessed                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Tasks to view              |
|                                   | supplementary evidence requested. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers may also choose to      |
|                                   | upload evidence to support the    |
|                                   | adverse impact of the disaster.   |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 19                                | Review scanned documents or       |
|                                   | evidence + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Have any documents or evidence    |
|                                   | been uploaded to support the      |
|                                   | claim?                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, to view the documents or     |
|                                   | evidence:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select links at the bottom of |
|                                   |     the expanded Claim Summary,   |
|                                   |     or                            |
|                                   | -   select [Quick link] from the  |
|                                   |     bottom of the open Process    |
|                                   |     Direct window, or             |
|                                   | -   select Documents from the     |
|                                   |     icon menu                     |
|                                   | -   go to Step 20                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 21                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 20                                | Review uploaded images + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer has uploaded        |
|                                   | evidence to show how they have    |
|                                   | been adversely impacted by the    |
|                                   | event, staff must check the       |
|                                   | agency’s false image repository   |
|                                   | and do a reverse image search.    |
|                                   | See Emergency payments -          |
|                                   | preventing fraud.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the image been identified as  |
|                                   | a false image?                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, the claim should be      |
|                                   |     reported, and then rejected   |
|                                   |     if approval to reject has     |
|                                   |     been given. See Table 7       |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 21             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 21                                | Identity Status + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if there are any concerns   |
|                                   | about the customer’s identity,    |
|                                   | see Table 7.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the TS screen, check the       |
|                                   | ‘Channel’ of the claim.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If it shows as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   WEB CHANNEL, this is an       |
|                                   |     online claim lodged by a      |
|                                   |     customer and the customer     |
|                                   |     will meet the identity        |
|                                   |     requirements, go to Step 22   |
|                                   | -   INTERNAL, this is a phone     |
|                                   |     claim lodged using ACC or a   |
|                                   |     claim form                    |
|                                   | -   If the customer:              |
|                                   |     - has a Confirmed identity    |
|                                   |     status, go to Step 22         |
|                                   |     - does not have a Confirmed   |
|                                   |     status, see Proof of identity |
|                                   |     requirements (POI) for        |
|                                   |     emergency payments, and then  |
|                                   |     return to this step           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 22                                | Concerns about the validity of    |
|                                   | information + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When assessing a claim, staff may |
|                                   | have concerns about the validity  |
|                                   | of the information. There may be  |
|                                   | warning signs that a claim may be |
|                                   | fraudulent. It may be an odd      |
|                                   | feeling or inconsistencies in     |
|                                   | what a customer claims.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the customer is      |
|                                   | showing behaviour that may        |
|                                   | suggest their claim is not valid. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This could be shown by, for       |
|                                   | example                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   a history of withdrawing      |
|                                   |     claims for AGDRP or NZ DRP    |
|                                   |     and/or different emergency    |
|                                   |     payments, including the       |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment, Disaster Recovery    |
|                                   |     Allowance (DRA) and New       |
|                                   |     Zealand Disaster Recovery     |
|                                   |     Allowance (NZ DRA)            |
|                                   | -   a DOA DOC relating to         |
|                                   |     concerns about fraud          |
|                                   | -   debt ACT DOCS completed on    |
|                                   |     record                        |
|                                   |     - Note: this is not a         |
|                                   |     complete list. Staff need to  |
|                                   |     consider details on the       |
|                                   |     customer’s record to          |
|                                   |     determine next steps.         |
|                                   | -   For help, contact Technical   |
|                                   |     Peer Support                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are no concerns about    |
|                                   | the validity of information, go   |
|                                   | to Step 23                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are concerns about the   |
|                                   | validity of information, before   |
|                                   | submitting a fraud report, first  |
|                                   | try to review the claim           |
|                                   | information and clarify any       |
|                                   | concerns with the customer, if    |
|                                   | appropriate. See Emergency        |
|                                   | payments - preventing fraud and   |
|                                   | Table 5                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After clarifying any concerns and |
|                                   | reviewing evidence (if            |
|                                   | applicable):                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the Service Officer is unsure  |
|                                   | whether to report a situation     |
|                                   | that they think may be suspected  |
|                                   | fraud, contact Technical Peer     |
|                                   | Support.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If fraud concerns have been       |
|                                   | resolved, continue processing the |
|                                   | claim, go to Step 23              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If fraud concerns have been       |
|                                   | resolved, but the evidence        |
|                                   | requested to validate discussions |
|                                   | has not been provided, and the    |
|                                   | timeframe to lodge evidence:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   has expired, the claim should |
|                                   |     be rejected. If approval has: |
|                                   |     - been given to reject        |
|                                   |     claims, process the claim,    |
|                                   |     see Table 2                   |
|                                   |     - not been given, place the   |
|                                   |     claim on hold, see Step 2 in  |
|                                   |     Table 3                       |
|                                   | -   has not expired, place the    |
|                                   |     claim On Hold for a further   |
|                                   |     28 days using hold reason     |
|                                   |     ‘Customer to Provide          |
|                                   |     information’. Procedure ends  |
|                                   |     here                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the Service Officer believes   |
|                                   | the customer has acted            |
|                                   | fraudulently:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Do not grant the claim        |
|                                   | -   See Table 7                   |

| 25                                | Claiming for a child/ren + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes. For all AGDRP claims go to   |
|                                   | Step 26.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For NZ DRP claims only            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer is eligible for NZ  |
|                                   | DRP and claiming for a child, the |
|                                   | child:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   does not need to be the       |
|                                   |     customer’s dependent child    |
|                                   | -   must live with the customer   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For more details, see NZ DRP      |
|                                   | claims only - ‘primary claimant’  |
|                                   | claims for a ‘secondary claimant. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is claiming for:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   a dependent child/ren, go to  |
|                                   |     Step 26                       |
|                                   | -   a child/ren who lives with    |
|                                   |     the customer but is not their |
|                                   |     dependent child, go to Step   |
|                                   |     29                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 26                                | Check principal carer status +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer is claiming for a   |
|                                   | biological child of a current     |
|                                   | relationship, a principal carer   |
|                                   | assessment is not needed. If the  |
|                                   | other parent disagrees with this  |
|                                   | decision, they can request a      |
|                                   | review and a principal carer      |
|                                   | assessment can be made as part of |
|                                   | that process. If children need to |
|                                   | be linked to a customer's record, |
|                                   | later steps will tell staff the   |
|                                   | process to follow depending if    |
|                                   | they are Families Shared Care     |
|                                   | trained.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select each child included in the |
|                                   | claim from the Relations [] menu. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In each child's record, review    |
|                                   | the following screens:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Child in Customer Care (CHC)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Shared Care Assessment (Families  |
|                                   | Shared Care and SSC Shared Care)  |
|                                   | (SCA)                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Child relationships (CHRE)        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The CHRE screen shows the     |
|                                   |     Relationship with the child   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the CHC screen shows the child |
|                                   | is in the care of the customer    |
|                                   | and there is:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   no percentage of care         |
|                                   |     recorded on the SCA screen,   |
|                                   |     however the child is recorded |
|                                   |     on the CHOC screen (in the    |
|                                   |     customer’s record, not the    |
|                                   |     child’s) with a Family Tax    |
|                                   |     Benefit or an income support  |
|                                   |     payment service reason, the   |
|                                   |     customer is considered a      |
|                                   |     principal carer for the       |
|                                   |     purposes of this claim        |
|                                   | -   a care percentage of 50% or   |
|                                   |     more on the FSC and SSC       |
|                                   |     tables for the child on the   |
|                                   |     SCA screen, the customer is   |
|                                   |     considered a principal carer  |
|                                   |     for the purposes of this      |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is not the        |
|                                   | principal carer of the child/ren, |
|                                   | note this for later. When         |
|                                   | processing the claim at Table 2,  |
|                                   | the child/ren will need to be     |
|                                   | unselected from the Eligible      |
|                                   | Dependent Child/ren table in the  |
|                                   | Disaster Recovery task selector.  |
|                                   | Go to Step 29                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the system show the customer |
|                                   | is the principal carer of the     |
|                                   | child/ren and the customer has    |
|                                   | not advised a change in care      |
|                                   | percentage in the claim of less   |
|                                   | than 50% care?                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 28            |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 27             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if staff have identified    |
|                                   | payment has been made to a person |
|                                   | who is not considered the         |
|                                   | principal carer of the child for  |
|                                   | the purposes of AGDRP, see Table  |
|                                   | 10.                               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

|                                   |                                   |

| 30                                | Referral of NZ DRP claims + Read  |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The claim needs to be finalised   |
|                                   | by staff with !FFAP access if a   |
|                                   | customer is claiming NZ DRP for:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   child/ren living with them    |
|                                   |     (not dependent child/ren)     |
|                                   | -   partner, and/or               |
|                                   | -   dependent adult               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have     |
|                                   | !FFAP access?                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Check the child’s CRN to see  |
|                                   |     if another person has already |
|                                   |     claimed for this child as the |
|                                   |     principal carer. If so, the   |
|                                   |     child will need to be removed |
|                                   |     as a secondary claimant from  |
|                                   |     the claim                     |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP claims with the above  |
|                                   |     secondary claimants cannot be |
|                                   |     finalised in Process Direct.  |
|                                   |     Pending future system         |
|                                   |     enhancements, continue to     |
|                                   |     review the claim to determine |
|                                   |     eligibility and payments to   |
|                                   |     be made. Go to Step 31        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Add any relevant information  |
|                                   |     already obtained or confirmed |
|                                   |     in the Progress of Claim      |
|                                   |     DL/Note to help the next      |
|                                   |     Service Officer               |
|                                   | -   Select Keyword icon           |
|                                   | -   Select Add button             |
|                                   | -   Key NOM in the keyword search |
|                                   |     field (this keyword is to be  |
|                                   |     used pending new keyword for  |
|                                   |     NZ DRP claims)                |
|                                   | -   Go to the Inbox in Process    |
|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   | -   In Main Category select WLM   |
|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   |     - Select Multi-Select         |
|                                   |     - Select the transaction from |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   |     - Select Unassign at the      |
|                                   |     bottom of the screen to       |
|                                   |     unassign the claim            |
|                                   |     - Select the Reason of Second |
|                                   |     contact attempt required      |
|                                   |     - Select Submit               |
|                                   | -   This will return NOM claims   |
|                                   |     to the allocation pool to be  |
|                                   |     reallocated to a trained      |
|                                   |     staff member                  |
|                                   | -   Do not put the claim on hold  |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 31                                | Child/ren not coded in care to    |
|                                   | cover date of impact of the       |
|                                   | disaster + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | At the ‘Is each dependent child   |
|                                   | linked to the customer’s record?’ |
|                                   | step did staff identify one or    |
|                                   | more child/ren are linked from a  |
|                                   | date that is after the date of    |
|                                   | impact of the disaster            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, payment will not issue for a |
|                                   | child if the date linked is after |
|                                   | the date of impact of the         |
|                                   | disaster                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Link must be updated outside  |
|                                   |     of the claim. Note: changing  |
|                                   |     child link dates inside the   |
|                                   |     claim will not give the       |
|                                   |     correct payment outcome.      |
|                                   | -   Take note of the customer's   |
|                                   |     Customer Reference Number and |
|                                   |     claim ID                      |
|                                   | -   Hold the claim for 2 days.    |
|                                   |     Note: not holding the claim   |
|                                   |     means the claim will not be   |
|                                   |     finalised and will allocate   |
|                                   |     to another Service Officer,   |
|                                   |     delaying a claim outcome for  |
|                                   |     the customer.                 |
|                                   |     - Select Status. Change it to |
|                                   |     On Hold and select any On     |
|                                   |     Hold Reason                   |
|                                   |     - Change the On Hold Expiry   |
|                                   |     Date to 2 days in the future  |
|                                   |     - Select Save and continue    |
|                                   |     with the below steps          |
|                                   | -   Exit the claim                |
|                                   |     - Select the Home icon to     |
|                                   |     exit the claim and return to  |
|                                   |     the Process Direct landing    |
|                                   |     page                          |
|                                   |     - Select the Customer Summary |
|                                   |     tile                          |
|                                   |     - Enter the customer’s CRN    |
|                                   |     and select search             |
|                                   |     - Key LS next to Super key    |
|                                   |     and press [Enter]             |
|                                   |     - Locate the correct          |
|                                   |     child/ren with ‘Link Type’ of |
|                                   |     CHI and click the pencil to   |
|                                   |     edit                          |
|                                   |     - Change the 'Start Date' to  |
|                                   |     the Event Date from the claim |
|                                   |     and save                      |
|                                   |     - Note: dates should not be   |
|                                   |     changed where this may impact |
|                                   |     other payments (such as FTB   |
|                                   |     or CCS) or where there are    |
|                                   |     shared care arrangements      |
|                                   |     which have not been           |
|                                   |     confirmed. For help, contact  |
|                                   |     Technical Peer Support        |
|                                   |     - Finalise the activity       |
|                                   |     - Navigate back to the        |
|                                   |     Process Direct landing page   |
|                                   |     - Click on Inbox, enter the   |
|                                   |     CRN and click Go              |
|                                   |     - Click on the claim to open  |
|                                   |     it                            |
|                                   |     - Click the Purple 'More      |
|                                   |     Actions' button and select    |
|                                   |     Regenerate                    |
|                                   |     - Continue processing claim.  |
|                                   |     Note: once the claim is       |
|                                   |     finalised, the claim will no  |
|                                   |     longer be on hold             |
|                                   |     - Go to Step 32               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 32                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 32                                | Nominee arrangements + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check if the customer has a       |
|                                   | current Nominee arrangement:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers who have not engaged    |
|                                   | with the agency for some time may |
|                                   | be unaware they have a current    |
|                                   | correspondence or payment nominee |
|                                   | arrangement.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | It is important to review these   |
|                                   | as sending payments or letters to |
|                                   | a nominee who is no longer valid  |
|                                   | could result in financial         |
|                                   | hardship or breach the customer’s |
|                                   | privacy.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff cannot check nominee        |
|                                   | information on the Nominee Link   |
|                                   | Summary (NOLS) screen in Process  |
|                                   | Direct. Staff should check the    |
|                                   | nominee information on the NOLS   |
|                                   | screen and Customer Summary in    |
|                                   | Customer First.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand to exit out of the      |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will go back to the  |
|                                   | Process Direct landing Page.      |
|                                   | Note: staff should not have the   |
|                                   | customer’s record open in         |
|                                   | Customer First and Process Direct |
|                                   | at the same time, as this can     |
|                                   | cause errors                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Customer First                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Next, type NOLS, Nominee       |
|                                   | arrangements will display as:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   NOP (Payment Nominee)         |
|                                   | -   NOC (Correspondence Nominee)  |
|                                   | -   NOB ( Correspondence and      |
|                                   |     Payment Nominee)              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer Summary in Customer      |
|                                   | First will show nominee           |
|                                   | information under Relationships   |
|                                   | and next to the Nominee: field.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Nominee: field will show      |
|                                   | nominee arrangements as follows:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   (pay) - if the customer has a |
|                                   |     payment nominee, or           |
|                                   | -   (corro) - if the customer has |
|                                   |     a correspondence nominee      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The NOLS screen may be coded with |
|                                   | a NOP, NOC or NOB however, if the |
|                                   | Nominee: field section is blank   |
|                                   | in the Customer Summary this      |
|                                   | means the customer is a nominee.  |
|                                   | That is, the customer does not    |
|                                   | have a nominee.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review nominee arrangements,      |
|                                   | including attempting to contact   |
|                                   | the customer if there are         |
|                                   | concerns of the currency of a     |
|                                   | voluntary arrangement (for        |
|                                   | example, arrangement is more than |
|                                   | 6 months old and the customer is  |
|                                   | not receiving a Centrelink        |
|                                   | payment)                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one attempt to contact the   |
|                                   | customer to discuss existing      |
|                                   | arrangements, and any other       |
|                                   | information that may be needed to |
|                                   | finalise their claim.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the contact attempt is         |
|                                   | unsuccessful:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Annotate the Progress of      |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document list/note  |
|                                   |     section with the contact      |
|                                   |     attempt and the information   |
|                                   |     that is needed from the       |
|                                   |     customer                      |
|                                   |     - Select Save                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close document       |
|                                   | -   Send a Q888 Request for       |
|                                   |     Customer to Contact letter    |
|                                   |     (do not send the Q164 letter  |
|                                   |     for emergency payments)       |
|                                   | -   Place the claim on hold for   |
|                                   |     14 days                       |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here until the |
|                                   |     customer makes contact to     |
|                                   |     discuss or the hold expires.  |
|                                   |     Then go to Step 6 Table 5     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the contact attempt is         |
|                                   | successful                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Ask the customer to give      |
|                                   |     Proof of Record Ownership     |
|                                   |     (PoRO). Do not give hints or  |
|                                   |     prompts that help the         |
|                                   |     customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   |     questions                     |
|                                   | -   Tell the customer their claim |
|                                   |     is being assessed. Confirm    |
|                                   |     with the customer where they  |
|                                   |     would like their payments to  |
|                                   |     be delivered, if the claim is |
|                                   |     eligible.                     |
|                                   | -   Annotate the Progress of      |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document list/note  |
|                                   |     section with the discussion   |
|                                   |     about the nominee arrangement |
|                                   |     - Select Save                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close document       |
|                                   | -   Cancel the nominee            |
|                                   |     arrangement if appropriate    |
|                                   |     following review and          |
|                                   |     discussion with the customer. |
|                                   |     Any nominee updates must be   |
|                                   |     completed in Customer First.  |
|                                   |     Staff not trained in          |
|                                   |     cancelling nominee            |
|                                   |     arrangements should contact   |
|                                   |     Technical Peer Support for    |
|                                   |     help                          |
|                                   | -   Continue assessing the claim  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Close the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Customer First. Return to the     |
|                                   | customer’s record in Process      |
|                                   | Direct.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer have a payment  |
|                                   | nominee arrangement?              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key ‘PAS’ next to Super Key   |
|                                   |     and press [Enter] to go to    |
|                                   |     the Payment Destination       |
|                                   |     Summary (PAS) screen          |
|                                   | -   Check for an FSP payment      |
|                                   | -   If there is:                  |
|                                   |     - an FSP payment, continue    |
|                                   |     assessing the claim, see      |
|                                   |     Table 2                       |
|                                   |     - no FSP payment, and trained |
|                                   |     in using the !FFAP screen,    |
|                                   |     see Table 8                   |
|                                   |     - no FSP payment and not      |
|                                   |     trained in using the !FFAP    |
|                                   |     screen, go to Step 33         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, see Table 2                   |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 33                                | Payment nominee, not !FFAP        |

|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   | -   Select the Reason of Second   |
|                                   |     contact attempt required      |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This will return NOM claims to    |
|                                   | the allocation pool to be         |
