Process claim

Table 2

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Select Process + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After completing all updates      |
|                                   | outside the claim, from the TS    |
|                                   | screen, select [more options] >   |
|                                   | Regenerate. This will make sure   |
|                                   | that all confirmed data is used   |
|                                   | when processing the claim.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Process at the bottom      |
|                                   | right of the claim to start       |
|                                   | assessing the claim.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The SAP Warnings and Messages     |
|                                   | (SWE) screen will display any     |
|                                   | errors or warnings relevant to    |
|                                   | the claim. Consider these during  |
|                                   | processing, but they are not the  |
|                                   | main focus of assessing the       |
|                                   | claim.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Message Log                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This section displays any errors  |
|                                   | with existing coding. These must  |
|                                   | be selected and resolved before   |
|                                   | the claim can be assessed. For    |
|                                   | help, see Using Digital Assistant |
|                                   | Roxy in Process Direct.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the error message              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | E044FF - Event Prerequisite not   |
|                                   | met shows, this means the         |
|                                   | customer has claimed for a        |
|                                   | concurrent event. These claims    |
|                                   | cannot be granted. Staff should   |
|                                   | have identified this in Table 1   |
|                                   | and escalated the claim           |
|                                   | accordingly.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | SR439 Customer in Environment I   |
|                                   | shows, the record is in           |
|                                   | Environment I. A claim processed  |
|                                   | in this environment will not      |
|                                   | finalise. If the customer is:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   not current on an income      |
|                                   |     support payment the record    |
|                                   |     must be transferred to the    |
|                                   |     local environment before      |
|                                   |     continuing. See Table 2 in    |
|                                   |     Process Direct navigation,    |
|                                   |     common screens and functions. |
|                                   |     For help, contact Technical   |
|                                   |     Peer Support. When the        |
|                                   |     environment transfer is       |
|                                   |     complete, continue the claim  |
|                                   |     process in Process Direct     |
|                                   | -   current on an income support  |
|                                   |     payment contact Technical     |
|                                   |     Peer Support who will         |
|                                   |     escalate to the Level 2       |
|                                   |     Helpdesk using the payment    |
|                                   |     query template                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer’s record must be     |
|                                   | transferred to the local          |
|                                   | environment before continuing.    |
|                                   | See Table 2 in Process Direct     |
|                                   | navigation, common screens and    |
|                                   | functions. For help, contact      |
|                                   | Technical Peer Support. When the  |
|                                   | environment transfer is complete, |
|                                   | continue the claim process in     |
|                                   | Process Direct.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Task Selectors                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These combine screens for a       |
|                                   | topic. A flag will display        |
|                                   | against Task Selectors or screens |
|                                   | that have provisional claim data. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These Task Selectors will         |
|                                   | pre-select for mandatory review:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Residency                     |
|                                   |     make sure the customer meets  |
|                                   |     the residence criteria        |
|                                   | -   Customer Detail Task Selector |
|                                   |     Staff can manually select     |
|                                   |     screens from the list if      |
|                                   |     needed                        |
|                                   | -   Payment Destination           |
|                                   |     If the customer receives      |
|                                   |     regular payments and provides |
|                                   |     a new account number that has |
|                                   |     not been recorded before,     |
|                                   |     confirmation may be required  |
|                                   |     to avoid ‘payment hijacking’  |
|                                   | -   Any screens that have         |
|                                   |     provisional data              |
|                                   | -   Disaster Recovery (all        |
|                                   |     screens)                      |
|                                   |     Some customer responses may   |
|                                   |     need to be changed after      |
|                                   |     pre-checks and assessment by  |
|                                   |     the Service Officer           |
|                                   |     The Disaster Recovery         |
|                                   |     workflow is listed last and   |
|                                   |     is be selected as mandatory.  |
|                                   |     This will make sure that      |
|                                   |     staff review all other        |
|                                   |     mandatory Task Sectors and    |
|                                   |     relevant screens before       |
|                                   |     completing the Disaster       |
|                                   |     Recovery workflow             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | At any time, staff can enter SWE  |
|                                   | next to Super key and press       |
|                                   | [Enter] to return to the Task     |
|                                   | Selector screen and select any of |
|                                   | the task selectors.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to go through         |
|                                   | selected screens.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: while the Super Key field   |
|                                   | can be used to review information |
|                                   | on specific screens, updates are  |
|                                   | not to be made directly to these  |
|                                   | screens. If updates are needed,   |
|                                   | return to the SWE screen, and     |
|                                   | select the relevant Task          |
|                                   | Selector. Make updates to the     |
|                                   | screen through the Task Selector. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See the Resources page for common |
|                                   | screens.                          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Disaster Recovery - Disaster      |
|                                   | Event + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure all other Task          |
|                                   | Selectors and screens have been   |
|                                   | reviewed before completing the    |
|                                   | Disaster Recovery screens.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Disaster Event                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Event Name: defaults to the event |
|                                   | selected by the customer and the  |
|                                   | payment (AGDRP or NZ DRP) based   |
|                                   | on the customer’s advice. This    |
|                                   | field cannot be changed.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For paper claims, take care to    |
|                                   | select the correct disaster event |
|                                   | and payment type from the         |
|                                   | dropdown menu.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: select the Previous button  |
|                                   | at any time in the Disaster       |
|                                   | Recovery workflow to view and     |
|                                   | update previous pages.            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | AGDRP / NZ DRP eligibility + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This screen prefills the details  |
|                                   | provided by the customer. Review  |
|                                   | their responses and record the    |
|                                   | correct response to each          |
|                                   | eligibility criteria, regardless  |
|                                   | of the customer's responses in    |
|                                   | the Claim Summary.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes or No as appropriate:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date claimant or dependent child  |
|                                   | impacted by the disaster event    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This is the date that a           |
|                                   | particular event or change of     |
|                                   | circumstance first affects a      |
|                                   | customer’s entitlement.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For example, when rising          |
|                                   | floodwaters first entered the     |
|                                   | customer's home.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Residency criteria                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the Residency Task         |
|                                   | Selector.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This includes screens to confirm  |
|                                   | a customer’s legal residence      |
|                                   | status, country of citizenship,   |
|                                   | New Zealand residence status and  |
|                                   | visa details.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The system may not automatically  |
|                                   | assess a customer’s residence     |
|                                   | status.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To avoid granting payments        |
|                                   | incorrectly, review all screens   |
|                                   | to make sure a customer meets the |
|                                   | residence criteria.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer does not need to be  |
|                                   | present in Australia at the time  |
|                                   | of making their claim.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check if the customer is a legal  |
|                                   | permanent Australian resident or  |
|                                   | holds a visa that qualifies them  |
|                                   | for AGDRP. Visas, and in some     |
|                                   | circumstances Australian          |
|                                   | citizenship, will show on the     |
|                                   | Legal Residence Details (RSLEG)   |
|                                   | screen. To check if a visa is a   |
|                                   | permanent visa, see Social        |
|                                   | Security Guide, Chapter 9.2, Visa |
|                                   | subclasses and payment            |
|                                   | eligibility for visas issued      |
|                                   | after 01/9/1994                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers may have 2 current      |
|                                   | visas showing on the RSLEG        |
|                                   | Screen, for example a 444 visa    |
|                                   | and a 010 visa.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must check the Residence    |
|                                   | Results Explanation Screen        |
|                                   | (RSREX) to check if the customer  |
|                                   | meets the residence criteria. See |
|                                   | AGDRP eligibility and NZ DRP      |
|                                   | eligibility in Eligibility for    |
|                                   | AGDRP and NZ DRP                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To do this:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key RSREX next to Super Key   |
|                                   |     and press [Enter]             |
|                                   | -   The RSREX screen will show    |
|                                   |     which visa is current.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: for NZ citizens (Visa Sub   |
|                                   | Class Code will be 444)           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Staff must carefully check    |
|                                   |     the New Zealand Residence     |
|                                   |     Status                        |
|                                   | -   Grandfathered (GRF) is a      |
|                                   |     protected Special Category    |
|                                   |     Visa (SCV) holder and should  |
|                                   |     apply for AGDRP, as an        |
|                                   |     Australian resident           |
|                                   | -   Transitional (TRA) is a       |
|                                   |     protected SCV holder and      |
|                                   |     should apply for AGDRP, as an |
|                                   |     Australian resident           |
|                                   | -   Not Entitled (NOT) is a       |
|                                   |     non-protected SCV holder and  |
|                                   |     should apply for NZ DRP       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if the customer should have |
|                                   | claimed AGDRP instead of NZ DRP   |
|                                   | or claimed NZ DRP instead of      |
|                                   | AGDRP, this should have been      |
|                                   | identified in Table 1. Return to  |
|                                   | the Customer has claimed the      |
|                                   | incorrect event or payment step   |
|                                   | in Table 1.                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Travel documents, such as         |
|                                   | passports, will show on the       |
|                                   | Immigration Enquiry (RSIMME)      |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer has travelled since |
|                                   | 1 September 1994, movement        |
|                                   | information should show on the    |
|                                   | Immigration Advised Movements     |
|                                   | (RSIM) screen                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A customer may have a successful  |
|                                   | immigration link but no movements |
|                                   | if they have a passport but have  |
|                                   | not travelled since 1 September   |
|                                   | 1994                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure the Country of          |
|                                   | Residence (CRES) screen is coded  |
|                                   | with the country a customer is    |
|                                   | currently living in. See          |
|                                   | Assessing if a customer is an     |
|                                   | Australian resident               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If it is identified the customer  |
|                                   | has claimed the incorrect payment |
|                                   | (that is, claimed AGDRP instead   |
|                                   | of NZ DRP or vice versa), the     |
|                                   | claim needs to be cancelled. See  |
|                                   | the Review claim details and      |
|                                   | check for previous claim step in  |
|                                   | Table 1.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is no details showing on |
|                                   | the RSIM, RSLEG, and/or RSIMME    |
|                                   | screens, request immigration      |
|                                   | data. On the RSIMME screen:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Request            |
|                                   |     Immigration Data button       |
|                                   | -   select Yes to continue        |
|                                   | -   once returned, the            |
|                                   |     information will show on the  |
|                                   |     relevant residence screens in |
|                                   |     the claim                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is an error or           |
|                                   | immigration details do not match, |
|                                   | see:                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Activating the Department of  |
|                                   |     Home Affairs datalink and     |
|                                   |     contingency procedures if     |
|                                   |     datalink is unavailable       |
|                                   | -   Referring inconsistencies in  |
|                                   |     overseas departure and        |
|                                   |     arrival information to        |
|                                   |     Centrelink International      |
|                                   |     Services (CIS)                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, contact Technical Peer  |
|                                   | Support.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer meet residence  |
|                                   | requirements?                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 4             |
|                                   | -   No, update the response to    |
|                                   |     'No' if needed. The customer  |
|                                   |     is not eligible and the claim |
|                                   |     is to be rejected. Selecting  |
|                                   |     Next will go to the Claim     |
|                                   |     Outcome screen. Go to Step 23 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date disaster impacted            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This date will prepopulate from   |
|                                   | the online claim. If an event end |
|                                   | date has been applied, the        |
|                                   | customer must meet all            |
|                                   | eligibility criteria on any day   |
|                                   | of that event, including age and  |
|                                   | address.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Refer to the event specific       |
|                                   | Operational Blueprint to confirm  |
|                                   | if an event end date has been     |
|                                   | applied. See Current emergency    |
|                                   | management events.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | End date applied:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the impact date within the     |
|                                   | event period?                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, this eligibility         |
|                                   |     criteria is met               |
|                                   | -   No, claim will need to be     |
|                                   |     rejected                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | End date not applied:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The date of impact advised by the |
|                                   | customer meets this eligibility   |
|                                   | criteria.                         |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Address during event + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The address advised by the        |
|                                   | customer in their claim will      |
|                                   | prefill. This may be their        |
|                                   | current address or they may       |
|                                   | advise they were living at a      |
|                                   | different address at the time of  |
|                                   | the disaster.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer updates their |
|                                   | address as part of the claim (at  |
|                                   | the ‘My Details’ section), this   |
|                                   | update will auto-complete (in     |
|                                   | most cases) and does not form     |
|                                   | part of the AGDRP/NZ DRA claim    |
|                                   | itself.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must use the Geospatial     |
|                                   | tool to determine if a customer   |
|                                   | lives within a disaster declared  |
|                                   | area. See the Operational         |
|                                   | Blueprint file for the current    |
|                                   | event being claimed to identify   |
|                                   | which areas have been declared.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the only impact reason a       |
|                                   | customer has selected in their    |
|                                   | claim is seriously injured or an  |
|                                   | immediate family member is        |
|                                   | deceased or missing, their        |
|                                   | address at the time of the        |
|                                   | disaster is not asked in the      |
|                                   | online claim and is not needed to |
|                                   | assess the claim.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Record the customer’s         |
|                                   |     confirmed home address on     |
|                                   |     this screen                   |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 10                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has selected      |
|                                   | seriously injured or an immediate |
|                                   | family member is deceased or      |
|                                   | missing and also indicated their  |
|                                   | home or major assets have been    |
|                                   | destroyed or damaged              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For claims lodged on or before 26 |
|                                   | March 2022, where authorised to   |
|                                   | make outbound calls, try to       |
|                                   | contact the customer to confirm   |
|                                   | their address at the time of the  |
|                                   | disaster. See Table 5 Step 2.     |
|                                   | Note: if not authorised to make   |
|                                   | outbound calls continue with the  |
|                                   | claim (later steps will show how  |
|                                   | to progress or escalate the claim |
|                                   | accordingly)                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the one genuine attempt to |
|                                   |     contact the customer is       |
|                                   |     successful or not successful, |
|                                   |     continue assessing the claim. |
|                                   |     Do not hold the claim at this |
|                                   |     point                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For claims lodged on or after 27  |
|                                   | March 2022, the above does not    |
|                                   | apply as the address at the time  |
|                                   | of the disaster will be asked     |
|                                   | where a customer also indicated   |
|                                   | their home or major assets have   |
|                                   | been destroyed or damaged         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Continue assessing these      |
|                                   |     claims                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the customer living in a      |
|                                   | declared area at the time of the  |
|                                   | disaster?                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 6             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 5              |
|                                   | -   Unsure, as the customer       |
|                                   |     lodged a claim on or before   |
|                                   |     26 March 2022 that indicated  |
|                                   |     they have been adversely      |
|                                   |     impacted due to Seriously     |
|                                   |     injured, Missing family       |
|                                   |     member or Deceased family     |
|                                   |     member, their home or major   |
|                                   |     assets have also been         |
|                                   |     destroyed or damaged, and     |
|                                   |     phone contact was             |
|                                   |     unsuccessful or could not be  |
|                                   |     made, go to Step 10           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Customer not living in a declared |
|                                   | area at time of disaster + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is not living in  |
|                                   | a declared area at the time of    |
|                                   | the disaster and the adverse      |
|                                   | impact(s) advised by the          |
|                                   | customer:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | includes destruction or damage of |
|                                   | home and/or major assets, the     |
|                                   | address within an impacted area   |
|                                   | should be recorded as No on the   |
|                                   | Eligibility screen (at Step 3).   |
|                                   | (If necessary, select Previous to |
|                                   | update response):                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   if either of these impacts    |
|                                   |     are not the only adverse      |
|                                   |     impacts declared, go to Step  |
|                                   |     10                            |
|                                   | -   if one or both of these       |
|                                   |     impacts are the only adverse  |
|                                   |     impacts declared, and the     |
|                                   |     customer does not live in a   |
|                                   |     declared area, the claim is   |
|                                   |     to be rejected. If approval   |
|                                   |     has:                          |
|                                   |     - been given to reject        |
|                                   |     claims, process the claim. Go |
|                                   |     to Step 24                    |
|                                   |     - not been given, see Step 2  |
|                                   |     in Table 3 to place the claim |
|                                   |     on hold                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | was only Seriously injured,       |
|                                   | Missing family member or Deceased |
|                                   | family member, the address within |
|                                   | an impacted area should be        |
|                                   | recorded as Yes on the            |
|                                   | Eligibility screen (at Step 3).   |
|                                   | Go to Step 10                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Address at time of disaster       |
|                                   | different to current address +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the Claim Summary.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To the question 'Address living   |
|                                   | at the time of the event?', did   |
|                                   | the customer advise a different   |
|                                   | address to their current address? |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, review the Address history   |
|                                   | by keying 'ADH' next to Super Key |
|                                   | and press [Enter]:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If both the current address   |
|                                   |     and address at the time of    |
|                                   |     the disaster are in a         |
|                                   |     declared area (as per the     |
|                                   |     Geospatial tool) for the same |
|                                   |     event, no further action is   |
|                                   |     required. Go to Step 10       |
|                                   | -   If the customer’s current     |
|                                   |     address is not in a declared  |
|                                   |     area (as per the Geospatial   |
|                                   |     tool), and they advised they  |
|                                   |     were living in a declared     |
|                                   |     area at the time of the       |
|                                   |     disaster, go to Step 7        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 10                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Review address history + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To determine whether additional   |
|                                   | evidence may be required to       |
|                                   | support the customer’s address at |
|                                   | the time of the disaster, locate  |
|                                   | the date the customer moved (DOV) |
|                                   | and the date the customer         |
|                                   | notified of the change (Date of   |
|                                   | Receipt = DOR).                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Open Customer First and access    |
|                                   | the customer’s record. Navigate   |
|                                   | to the Address History screen by  |
|                                   | keying ADH in the Next field then |
|                                   | Enter                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note the Activity Management      |
|                                   | Reference Number(s) (AMR) for the |
|                                   | address(es) to be reviewed        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Clear Customer from Customer      |
|                                   | First                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Process Direct go to the Event |
|                                   | Summary screen by entering ES     |
|                                   | next to Super Key and press       |
|                                   | [Enter]                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter the AMR number(s) in the    |
|                                   | Activity ID field                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Note: If the activity is 90   |
|                                   |     days or older, search for     |
|                                   |     archived activity history     |
|                                   |     using the Archiving and       |
|                                   |     Culling Engine (ACE) via the  |
|                                   |     Intranet. See                 |
|                                   |     Using the Archiving and       |
|                                   |     Culling Engine (ACE) to       |
|                                   |     access archived Activity      |
|                                   |     Management History (AMHS)     |
|                                   |     data. For help, contact       |
|                                   |     Technical Peer Support.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select View Details to display    |
|                                   | the Activity Details. The Date of |
|                                   | receipt (the date the update was  |
|                                   | notified) is located under the    |
|                                   | Additional activity details       |
|                                   | column                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Take note of the DOV and the DOR  |
|                                   | for each address to be reviewed   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Also identify any short periods   |
|                                   | the customers moved from a        |
|                                   | non-declared area to a declared   |
|                                   | area (for example, moved to a     |
|                                   | declared area for 4 weeks)        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are concerns a customer  |
|                                   | may be retrospectively providing  |
|                                   | false address details so it       |
|                                   | appears they live in a declared   |
|                                   | disaster area, see Conduct an     |
|                                   | address search in                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Emergency payments - preventing   |
|                                   | fraud and                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Table 7.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the address at the time of the |
|                                   | disaster recorded on the ADH      |
|                                   | screen?                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, and the Start Date (DOV) of  |
|                                   | the customer’s current address is |
|                                   | before the disaster event start   |
|                                   | date and the address was updated: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   before the disaster, go to    |
|                                   |     step 10                       |
|                                   | -   after the disaster event      |
|                                   |     start date and the customer   |
|                                   |     is not receiving an income    |
|                                   |     support payment, go to Step 9 |
|                                   | -   after the disaster event      |
|                                   |     start date and the customer   |
|                                   |     is receiving an income        |
|                                   |     support payment, go to Step 8 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 9                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Check for evidence for ISP        |
|                                   | customers + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | ISP customers are generally       |
|                                   | required to provide evidence of a |
|                                   | change of address, particularly   |
|                                   | where they receive Rent           |
|                                   | Assistance.                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check for evidence of the change  |
|                                   | of address(es) being reviewed.    |
|                                   | Select [Quick link] and find any  |
|                                   | documents uploaded in the last 14 |
|                                   | days or after the DOV. For        |
|                                   | example, a rent certificate or    |
|                                   | lease agreement. This may be used |
|                                   | to validate the customer’s        |
|                                   | address(es) without further       |
|                                   | contact.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the DOV and DOR identified  |
|                                   | for the address(es) at Step 7,    |
|                                   | determine when the customer       |
|                                   | notified of their change of       |
|                                   | address.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Did the ISP customer:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | advise of a change of address     |
|                                   | starting on or before the         |
|                                   | disaster start event date (that   |
|                                   | is the DOV is on or before the    |
|                                   | disaster event start date) or     |
|                                   | they moved during the disaster    |
|                                   | period, and                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | they notified more than 14 days   |
|                                   | after the start date of the       |
|                                   | address (that is, the DOR is more |
|                                   | than 14 days after the DOV)?      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes:                          |
|                                   |     If sufficient evidence has    |
|                                   |     been provided, for example    |
|                                   |     the customer has uploaded a   |
|                                   |     rent certificate or rental    |
|                                   |     agreement, go to Step 10      |
|                                   |     If evidence has not been      |
|                                   |     provided, the customer has    |
|                                   |     not met the requirements for  |
|                                   |     the income support payment    |
|                                   |     they are receiving. If        |
|                                   |     approval has:                 |
|                                   |     - been given to reject        |
|                                   |     claims, process the claim. Go |
|                                   |     to Step 24                    |
|                                   |     - not been given, place claim |
|                                   |     on hold. See Step 2 in Table  |
|                                   |     3                             |
|                                   | -   No, additional evidence is    |
|                                   |     not required (as the customer |
|                                   |     notified within their         |
|                                   |     required reporting            |
|                                   |     timeframe). Go to Step 10     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Contact the customer to request   |
|                                   | evidence of address + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS only) between 8:00 am and    |
|                                   | 8:00 pm using the customer's      |
|                                   | local time, to let them know a    |
|                                   | Service Officer will call them    |
|                                   | today from a private number.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer to request   |
|                                   | evidence of their address at the  |
|                                   | time of the disaster.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer needs an      |
|                                   | interpreter, the 4 digit office   |
|                                   | code ID is 1897 for Smart Centre  |
|                                   | Emergency Management. See         |
|                                   | Contacting an on-demand telephone |
|                                   | interpreter (Interpreter          |
|                                   | Connect).                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If contact was successful         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ask the customer to give Proof of |
|                                   | Record Ownership (PoRO). Do not   |
|                                   | give hints or prompts that help   |
|                                   | the customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   | questions                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Read the verbal request statement |
|                                   | for AGDRP/NZ DRP                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ask the customer to provide       |
|                                   | evidence of their address at the  |
|                                   | time of the disaster. For         |
|                                   | example, a current rental         |
|                                   | agreement, utility bill, bank     |
|                                   | statement, or drivers licence     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note on the DL screen under the   |
|                                   | Document list/note section with   |
|                                   | the outcome of the discussion     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select Close document         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If requested, encourage them to   |
|                                   | upload documents through the      |
|                                   | requested task in their online    |
|                                   | claim on the day. This will allow |
|                                   | their claim to be processed as    |
|                                   | soon as possible                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer agreed to the    |
|                                   | verbal request?                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, see Step 3 in Table 5    |
|                                   | -   No, see Step 4 in Table 5     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If contact was not successful     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Step 4 in Table 5.            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 10                                | Is the customer claiming NZ       |
|                                   | DRP? + Read more ...              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 12            |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 11             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 11                                | AGDRP dependent children          |
|                                   | details + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Did the customer claim for        |
|                                   | dependent children?               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Review the Eligible dependent |
|                                   |     child/children details table. |
|                                   |     Make sure the customer is the |
|                                   |     principal carer of all        |
|                                   |     children and any care         |
|                                   |     reassessments have been       |
|                                   |     undertaken as per the         |
|                                   |     pre-checks in Table 1         |
|                                   | -   If any child listed in the    |
|                                   |     table has been assessed as    |
|                                   |     not eligible due to existing  |
|                                   |     principal carer coding, or    |
|                                   |     because the partner has       |
|                                   |     previously been paid for this |
|                                   |     event for this child,         |
|                                   |     unselect them from the claim. |
|                                   |     Note: this should have been   |
|                                   |     identified in Table 1         |
|                                   | -   Take note of any child/ren    |
|                                   |     unselected. This is to record |
|                                   |     details and why they are not  |
|                                   |     eligible in the Claim         |
|                                   |     Finalisation Note             |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 14                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 14                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 12                                | NZ DRP secondary claimant(s) +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer is advised of the    |
|                                   | definition of a secondary         |
|                                   | claimant when completing the      |
|                                   | online claim or ACC. Where the    |
|                                   | customer has claimed for a        |
|                                   | secondary claimant this can be    |
|                                   | accepted without further          |
|                                   | evidence.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the claimant want to claim   |
|                                   | for a secondary claimant?         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, review the Dependent         |
|                                   | adult(s) and child/children       |
|                                   | details table:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Make sure any child/ren where |
|                                   |     customer is not principal     |
|                                   |     carer has not been paid under |
|                                   |     a claim made by a principal   |
|                                   |     carer of this child           |
|                                   | -   Make sure all secondary       |
|                                   |     claimants (including claims   |
|                                   |     for a dependent child, child  |
|                                   |     living with the customer,     |
|                                   |     partner, or dependent adult)  |
|                                   |     meet the eligibility criteria |
|                                   | -   If any person listed on the   |
|                                   |     table has been assessed as    |
|                                   |     not eligible, unselect them   |
|                                   |     from the claim                |
|                                   | -   Take note of any secondary    |
|                                   |     claimants unselected. Details |
|                                   |     of why a child or secondary   |
|                                   |     claimant were removed from    |
|                                   |     the claim will need to be     |
|                                   |     included in the Claim Note    |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 13                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 13                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 13                                | NZ DRP - participation in tax     |
|                                   | system + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Before an NZ DRP claim can be     |
|                                   | granted, customers need to        |
|                                   | provide evidence they are or will |
|                                   | be participating in the           |
|                                   | Australian tax system.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When submitting the claim, where  |
|                                   | customers:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   correctly selected to claim   |
|                                   |     NZ DRP, they are asked to     |
|                                   |     provide this information and  |
|                                   |     advised their claim cannot be |
|                                   |     assessed until they provided  |
|                                   |     it                            |
|                                   | -   incorrectly selected to claim |
|                                   |     AGDRP (this would have been   |
|                                   |     identified at the Customer    |
|                                   |     claimed the incorrect event   |
|                                   |     or payment step in Table 1),  |
|                                   |     these customers must be       |
|                                   |     contacted to request evidence |
|                                   |     of their participation in the |
|                                   |     Australian taxation system.   |
|                                   |     This is because they were not |
|                                   |     prompted to do so when        |
|                                   |     claiming AGDRP. Go to Table 5 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, see the eligibility     |
|                                   | criteria.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | NZ DRP cannot be granted until    |
|                                   | this evidence has been provided.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer provided         |
|                                   | evidence to demonstrate tax       |
|                                   | participation?                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Make sure to select the       |
|                                   |     correct tax participation     |
|                                   |     criteria                      |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 14                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, place the claim on hold and   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note on the DL screen under the   |
|                                   | Document list/note section to say |
|                                   | why the claim is on hold. See     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Step 5 in Table 5                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 14                                | Living in Australia + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This page indicates whether the   |
|                                   | customer was living in Australia: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   at the time of the disaster,  |

|                                   | -   at the time of lodging the    |
|                                   |     claim                         |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   does not need to be in        |
|                                   |     Australia at the time of the  |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     there                         |

|                                   |                                   |

| 18                                | Injury to themselves or a         |
|                                   | dependent + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Dependent adult(s) and        |
|                                   | child(ren) injury details page    |
|                                   | lists details of any child(ren)   |
|                                   | being claimed, and any dependent  |
|                                   | adult(s) (including partners) for |
|                                   | NZ DRP customers. If not injured, |
|                                   | information about how they were   |
|                                   | impacted by the disaster is also  |
|                                   | recorded.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, see eligibility         |
|                                   | criteria.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review details of claims made to  |
|                                   | serious injury to the customer,   |
|                                   | their dependent child, or         |
|                                   | secondary claimant (NZ DRP).      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has indicated     |
|                                   | there was no hospitalisation, and |
|                                   | has not met adversely impacted    |
|                                   | criteria for any other reason,    |
|                                   | contact the customer to find out  |
|                                   | if the person would have been     |
|                                   | admitted to hospital under normal |
|                                   | circumstances.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Can the claim be assessed without |
|                                   | further information from the      |
|                                   | customer?                         |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     adult(s) and child(ren)       |
|                                   |     injury details table          |
|                                   |     accordingly, then go to Step  |
|                                   |     20                            |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 19             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 19                                | Contact the customer about the    |
|                                   | serious injury + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS only) between 8:00 am and    |
|                                   | 8:00 pm using the customer's      |
|                                   | local time, to let them know a    |
|                                   | Service Officer will call them    |
|                                   | today from a private number.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer about the    |
|                                   | injury.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer needs an      |
|                                   | interpreter, the 4 digit office   |
|                                   | code ID is 1897 for Smart Centre  |
|                                   | Emergency Management. See         |
|                                   | Contacting an on-demand telephone |
|                                   | interpreter (Interpreter          |
|                                   | Connect).                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If contact was successful         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Ask the customer to give      |
|                                   |     Proof of Record Ownership     |
|                                   |     (PoRO). Do not give hints or  |
|                                   |     prompts that help the         |
|                                   |     customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   |     questions                     |
|                                   | -   Ask the customer about the    |
|                                   |     nature of the injuries and if |
|                                   |     they would have been admitted |
|                                   |     to hospital if not for the    |
|                                   |     disaster event                |
|                                   | -   If evidence is not available, |
|                                   |     a declaration by the customer |
|                                   |     may be accepted. Contact      |
|                                   |     Technical Peer Support if no  |
|                                   |     evidence is available or if   |
|                                   |     it is unclear whether the     |
|                                   |     customer meets the criteria.  |
|                                   |     They will escalate the claim  |
|                                   |     to the Level 2 Helpdesk       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Are the injury criteria met?      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, Update the Injured or        |
|                                   | missing person(s) screen          |
|                                   | accordingly. Go to Step 20        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Tell the customer their claim |
|                                   |     cannot be granted, as they do |
|                                   |     not meet the qualification    |
|                                   |     for the payment. They will be |
|                                   |     notified of the outcome. Tell |
|                                   |     them of their review and      |
|                                   |     appeal rights                 |
|                                   | -   The claim should be rejected. |
|                                   |     If approval has:              |
|                                   |     - been given to reject        |
|                                   |     claims, process the claim. Go |
|                                   |     to Step 24                    |
|                                   |     - not been given, place claim |
|                                   |     on hold. See Step 2 in Table  |
|                                   |     3                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If contact was not successful     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Send a Request for Information.   |
|                                   | See Step 4 in Table 5.            |
