| 24                                | Claim Decision + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer meets all other   |
|                                   | eligibility criteria, and it was  |
|                                   | identified at the Review claim    |
|                                   | details step in Table 1, that     |
|                                   | customer contact is needed to     |
|                                   | further discuss free text         |
|                                   | information and confirm if a      |
|                                   | valid (eligible) impact reason is |
|                                   | met, go to Table 5.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Otherwise, complete the Claim     |
|                                   | Outcome details before finalising |
|                                   | the claim.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claim outcome                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the relevant outcome based |
|                                   | on the assessment of the claim:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Grant if:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the customer does or does not |
|                                   |     meet identity requirements    |
|                                   |     for the payment, and          |
|                                   | -   there are no concerns about   |
|                                   |     the validity of the           |
|                                   |     customer’s claim or their     |
|                                   |     identity, and                 |
|                                   | -   they meet all other           |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria          |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 25                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reject if the customer does not   |
|                                   | meet the core eligibility         |
|                                   | criteria and/or there was         |
|                                   | insufficient information to make  |
|                                   | an assessment. For example,       |
|                                   | evidence was not provided within  |
|                                   | the time frame requested. See     |
|                                   | Step 1 In Table 3                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 25                                | Payment Components + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This table will present when the  |
|                                   | claim outcome is Grant.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | It lists the payments to be made  |
|                                   | to the customer, and any          |
|                                   | dependent children.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Carefully review the table to     |
|                                   | make sure all parties have been   |
|                                   | assessed as entitled to a         |
|                                   | payment. For example, the         |
|                                   | customer is the principal carer   |
|                                   | of the child/ren, the partner has |
|                                   | not already been paid or claimed  |
|                                   | a payment in their own right (NZ  |
|                                   | DRP only).                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If they are not entitled          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Previous to return to  |
|                                   |     the dependent child table and |
|                                   | -   unselect them from the claim  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Payments are $1000 per adult and  |
|                                   | $400 per child.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Payment options                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Immediate payment: defaults   |
|                                   |     to Yes as payments are made   |
|                                   |     via the New Payment Platform  |
|                                   | -   Method of payment: defaults   |
|                                   |     to Priority Direct Credit     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Payment by instalments is not an  |
|                                   | option for AGDRP. NPP will        |
|                                   | deliver the payment in full.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Step 4 in Table 3.            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Assess and finalise claim

Table 3

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | AGDRP/ NZ DRP claim to be         |
|                                   | rejected + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If not rejecting the claim, go to |
|                                   | Step 4.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claims cannot be rejected until   |
|                                   | formal approval is provided.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Rejecting claims in the       |
|                                   | Operational Blueprint for the     |
|                                   | event.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Approval may be given to reject   |
|                                   | claims for specific reasons       |
|                                   | during the life of an active      |
|                                   | event.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Before rejecting any claim, staff |
|                                   | must check the claim and any Note |
|                                   | or DOC on the customer’s record   |
|                                   | to make sure the customer is not  |
|                                   | eligible. Staff must determine if |
|                                   | the claim should be granted or    |
|                                   | rejected.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For:                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The New South Wales Floods – July |
|                                   | 2022, South East Queensland       |
|                                   | Floods - February 2022 and New    |
|                                   | South Wales Floods - February     |
|                                   | 2022, staff must carefully check: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   reasons claims can be         |
|                                   |     rejected, and                 |
|                                   | -   the LGAs where, before        |
|                                   |     finalising a claim            |
|                                   |     - The claim must be allocated |
|                                   |     to a specialist team to       |
|                                   |     contact the customer and      |
|                                   |     finalise the claim            |
|                                   |     - 2 genuine attempts to       |
|                                   |     contact the customer must be  |
|                                   |     made                          |
|                                   |     - 1 attempt to contact the    |
|                                   |     customer must be made         |
|                                   |     - no attempts to contact the  |
|                                   |     customer are needed           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Carefully check the LGA claimed.  |
|                                   | See Map of affected areas in the  |
|                                   | Resources page of:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   New South Wales Floods – July |
|                                   |     2022                          |
|                                   | -   South East Queensland Floods  |
|                                   |     – February 2022               |
|                                   | -   New South Wales Floods –      |
|                                   |     February 2022                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is there formal approval to       |
|                                   | reject claims for the payment     |
|                                   | type (AGDRP or NZ DRP) and        |
|                                   | reason, and has the customer’s    |
|                                   | claim and any relevant DOCs been  |
|                                   | checked to make sure the customer |
|                                   | is not eligible?                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   if a DOA DOC on record        |
|                                   |     identifies a claim as ‘not    |
|                                   |     genuine’ customer contact is  |
|                                   |     not needed, as information on |
|                                   |     the record has been deemed by |
|                                   |     a Fraud Analyst to not be     |
|                                   |     legitimate or belonging to    |
|                                   |     the customer. These claims    |
|                                   |     will also have the keyword    |
|                                   |     FRDREJ listed. Go to Step 4   |
|                                   | -   if the Operational Blueprint  |
|                                   |     for the event advises         |
|                                   |     - no customer contact is      |
|                                   |     needed, go to Step 4          |
|                                   |     - customer contact is needed  |
|                                   |     by a specialist team and the  |
|                                   |     Service Officer assessing the |
|                                   |     claim needs to allocate the   |
|                                   |     claim to this team to         |
|                                   |     finalise,  go to Step 7       |
|                                   |     - customer contact is needed  |
|                                   |     and the claim does not need   |
|                                   |     to be allocated to a          |
|                                   |     specialist team, go to Step 3 |
|                                   | -   if the Operational Blueprint  |
|                                   |     for the event does not have   |
|                                   |     specific details about        |
|                                   |     customer contact, 2 genuine   |
|                                   |     attempts to contact the       |
|                                   |     customer must be made, go to  |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 2                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Place the claim on hold + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update Claim Status               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Status, change it to   |
|                                   |     On Hold and select the        |
|                                   |     appropriate On Hold Reason.   |
|                                   |     See the Resources page for a  |
|                                   |     list                          |
|                                   | -   Change the On Hold Expiry     |
|                                   |     Date to 28 days in the future |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note on the DL screen under the   |
|                                   | Document list/note section        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Record details of why the     |
|                                   |     claim is to be rejected and   |
|                                   |     why it is on hold. Do not use |
|                                   |     the term 'fraud' on the       |
|                                   |     customer's record if the      |
|                                   |     record has been referred for  |
|                                   |     review                        |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select Close document         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When the hold period ends, the    |
|                                   | claim will return to the pool to  |
|                                   | be allocated for processing. It   |
|                                   | will be reassessed, taking into   |
|                                   | account the information in the    |
|                                   | Progress of Claim Note on the DL  |
|                                   | screen under the Document         |
|                                   | list.note section. Make sure to   |
|                                   | record all information about why  |
|                                   | the claim was placed on hold.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Customer contact for unfavourable |
|                                   | decisions + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Before finalising the claim,      |
|                                   | check the contact requirements    |
|                                   | for unfavourable decisions for    |
|                                   | the relevant event or reason. See |
|                                   | Rejecting claims in the           |
|                                   | Operational Blueprint for the     |
|                                   | event.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For the New South Wales Floods –  |
|                                   | July 2022, South East Queensland  |
|                                   | Floods - February 2022 and New    |
|                                   | South Wales Floods - February     |
|                                   | 2022, carefully check when:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   a claim needs to be allocated |
|                                   |     to a specialist team to       |
|                                   |     contact the customer and      |
|                                   |     finalise the claim. Staff not |
|                                   |     in this specialist team,      |
|                                   |     refer the claim to the        |
|                                   |     specialist team. Go to Step 7 |
|                                   | -   2 genuine attempts to contact |
|                                   |     the customer must be made.    |
|                                   |     This depends on the LGA.      |
|                                   |     Continue with this step       |
|                                   | -   one attempt to contact the    |
|                                   |     customer must be made,        |
|                                   |     continue with this step       |
|                                   | -   no contact is required. This  |
|                                   |     depends on the reason for     |
|                                   |     rejection. Go to Step 4       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the Operational Blueprint for  |
|                                   | the event does not have specific  |
|                                   | details about customer contact, 2 |
|                                   | genuine attempts to contact the   |
|                                   | customer must be made. Continue   |
|                                   | with this step.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification SMS |
|                                   | only between 8:00 am and 8:00 pm  |
|                                   | using the customer's local time,  |
|                                   | to let them know a Service        |
|                                   | Officer will call them today from |
|                                   | a private number.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Successful contact                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help in in making outbound    |
|                                   | calls see the Training & Support  |
|                                   | page for a link to Telephony      |
|                                   | contact guides (inbound and       |
|                                   | outbound) > Outbound contact      |
|                                   | guide - ineligible claims.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ask the customer to give Proof of |
|                                   | Record Ownership (PoRO). Do not   |
|                                   | give hints or prompts that help   |
|                                   | the customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   | questions.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the customer’s claim      |
|                                   | details. Allow them to update     |
|                                   | these if their circumstances have |
|                                   | changed as this may make them     |
|                                   | eligible for payment.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer now meets the     |
|                                   | eligibility criteria, process the |
|                                   | claim and provide the customer an |
|                                   | outcome during the call. This     |
|                                   | includes where the customer can   |
|                                   | upload evidence to support their  |
|                                   | claim and they can do this while  |
|                                   | on the phone for staff to assess  |
|                                   | during the call. To grant the     |
|                                   | claim, go to Step 4.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer still does not    |
|                                   | meet the eligibility criteria,    |
|                                   | including being unable to upload  |
|                                   | any evidence now to support their |
|                                   | claim while on the phone, tell    |
|                                   | them:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the reason for the ineligible     |
|                                   | claim (Do not use the term        |
|                                   | rejection or rejected claim) This |
|                                   | includes where rejection is due   |
|                                   | to concerns about their identity, |
|                                   | adverse impacts claimed or false  |
|                                   | image/s uploaded. For example, if |
|                                   | the rejection is because of:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   concerns about validity of    |
|                                   |     identity or details in the    |
|                                   |     claim, say                    |
|                                   |     'the claim cannot be granted  |
|                                   |     due to concerns about the     |
|                                   |     validity of the details       |
|                                   |     provided, so eligibility      |
|                                   |     cannot be established'        |
|                                   | -   uploaded false image/s, say   |
|                                   |     'the image/s uploaded were    |
|                                   |     found on the internet and do  |
|                                   |     not support the claim for     |
|                                   |     major damage'                 |
|                                   | -   do not tell the customer      |
|                                   |     their claim is unsuccessful   |
|                                   |     due to possible fraud or was  |
|                                   |     referred for a fraud          |
|                                   |     assessment. Do not use the    |
|                                   |     term 'fraud’ when speaking to |
|                                   |     the customer or updating the  |
|                                   |     customer's record             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a notice of decision will be sent |
|                                   | to them                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | their appeal rights               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to visit the Help in an emergency |
|                                   | page for more information and use |
|                                   | the Payment and Service Finder to |
|                                   | check which claim is suitable for |
|                                   | them                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the customer may be        |
|                                   |     eligible for Disaster         |
|                                   |     Recovery Allowance (DRA) or   |
|                                   |     New Zealand Disaster Recovery |
|                                   |     Allowance (NZ DRA), see       |
|                                   |     Claiming emergency payments   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Customers seeking information |
|                                   |     about state government        |
|                                   |     grants, housing and           |
|                                   |     accommodation, health and     |
|                                   |     wellbeing, clean-up and waste |
|                                   |     removal, managing             |
|                                   |     contamination and material    |
|                                   |     help can be directed to their |
|                                   |     local evacuation/recovery     |
|                                   |     centre                        |
|                                   |     See Resources page for        |
|                                   |     Disasters (community support  |
|                                   |     Queensland) and Disasters     |
|                                   |     (community support New South  |
|                                   |     Wales)                        |
|                                   | -   Customers who require         |
|                                   |     personal support and          |
|                                   |     counselling should be         |
|                                   |     warm-transferred to the       |
|                                   |     Social Work Disaster Line.    |
|                                   |     Please be clear that social   |
|                                   |     workers cannot change payment |
|                                   |     decisions. See Referring a    |
|                                   |     customer during a declared    |
|                                   |     disaster or emergency         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 4.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Unsuccessful contact              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the Operational Blueprint for  |
|                                   | the event advises only 1 attempt  |
|                                   | to contact the customer is        |
|                                   | needed, go to Step 4              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If 2 genuine attempts to contact  |
|                                   | the customer are needed:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | First unsuccessful attempt: Place |
|                                   | the claim On Hold for 1 business  |
|                                   | day with On hold reason ‘Pending  |
|                                   | customer contact’.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Annotate the Progress of      |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document            |
|                                   |     list/notes.section            |
|                                   |     - Select Save                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close document       |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Second unsuccessful attempt:      |
|                                   | There is no need to attempt       |
|                                   | further outbound calls once the 2 |
|                                   | genuine attempts have been made   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure the details of both     |
|                                   | contact attempts (phone           |
|                                   | number(s), date(s) and time(s) of |
|                                   | each attempt) are recorded in the |
|                                   | Claim Finalisation Note.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 4.                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Assess claim + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete the Claim Decision       |
|                                   | screen with the correct outcome.  |
|                                   | For ineligible claims, staff      |
|                                   | should select the most            |
|                                   | appropriate ineligible            |
|                                   | (rejection) reason from the       |
|                                   | hierarchy of ineligible           |
|                                   | (rejection) reasons.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When rejecting claims, do not     |
|                                   | update any of the claim           |
|                                   | assessment screens in Process     |
|                                   | Direct apart from the Claim       |
|                                   | Decision screen                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must record the reason for  |
|                                   | decision:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to return to the SAP  |
|                                   | Warnings and Messages (SWE)       |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Assess button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Resolve any errors that may       |
|                                   | present on the SWE screen. For    |
|                                   | help, see Using Digital Assistant |
|                                   | Roxy in Process Direct            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the E027FY error shows on the  |
|                                   | SWE screen, if the customer is    |
|                                   | subscribed, issue a pre-call      |
|                                   | notification (SMS) to the         |
|                                   | customer between 8:00 am and 8:00 |
|                                   | pm using the customer's local     |
|                                   | time to let them know a Service   |
|                                   | Officer will call them today from |
|                                   | a private number                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer to discuss   |
|                                   | their family income estimate      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Contact successful            |
|                                   |     - Ask the customer to give    |
|                                   |     Proof of Record Ownership     |
|                                   |     (PoRO). Do not give hints or  |
|                                   |     prompts that help the         |
|                                   |     customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   |     questions                     |
|                                   |     - Families trained staff -    |
|                                   |     update the customer’s record  |
|                                   |     with an income estimate for   |
|                                   |     the current financial year    |
|                                   |     - Not Families trained        |
|                                   |     staff - contact the F&P       |
|                                   |     Payment Queries TPS via       |
|                                   |     Services Australia Workspace  |
|                                   |     or 177111 for help            |
|                                   | -   Contact unsuccessful, go to   |
|                                   |     Step 8                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After fixing any errors, select   |
|                                   | Assess again to go to the         |
|                                   | Entitlements (ELD) screen         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If granting or rejecting the      |
|                                   | claim, is the claim generating    |
|                                   | arrears or debts for AGDRP or any |
|                                   | other payments?                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 5             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 6              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Claim generating arrears/debts    |
|                                   | for other payments + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not finalise the AGDRP/ NZ DRP |
|                                   | claim until the outcome has been  |
|                                   | investigated and confirmed as     |
|                                   | correct, or until corrective      |
|                                   | action taken if needed.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the reason for the arrears/   |
|                                   | debt been identified?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, and the outcome is:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   correct, record the reason    |
|                                   |     for the arrears or debts in   |
|                                   |     the Claim Finalisation Note.  |
|                                   |     Go to Step 6                  |
|                                   | -   not correct but can be fixed, |
|                                   |     make the required updates to  |
|                                   |     correct the outcome. Record   |
|                                   |     details of updates and any    |
|                                   |     arrears or debts (if          |
|                                   |     applicable) in the Claim      |
|                                   |     Finalisation Note. Go to Step |
|                                   |     6                             |
|                                   | -   not correct but unsure what   |
|                                   |     action is needed, escalate    |
|                                   |     the record as appropriate. If |
|                                   |     necessary, contact Technical  |
|                                   |     Peer Support. Procedure ends  |
|                                   |     here, pending confirmation    |
|                                   |     the outcome is correct or     |
|                                   |     corrective coding is required |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, follow the usual escalation   |
|                                   | process. If necessary, seek       |
|                                   | support from a TPS. Procedure     |
|                                   | ends here, pending confirmation   |
|                                   | the outcome is correct or         |
|                                   | corrective coding is required     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Finalise claim + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer does not meet the   |
|                                   | eligibility criteria for more     |
|                                   | than one reason, document all     |
|                                   | reasons and the reason why the    |
|                                   | ineligible reason was selected    |
|                                   | from the hierarchy of ineligible  |
|                                   | (rejection) reasons. The reason   |
|                                   | selected will determine what      |
|                                   | information is advised in the     |
|                                   | outcome letter.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once the claim is assessed        |
|                                   | correctly, and relevant attempts  |
|                                   | (if needed) have been made to     |
|                                   | contact the customer of an        |
|                                   | unfavourable decision, select     |
|                                   | Finish.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claim Finalisation Note will  |
|                                   | appear.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Recording reasons for         |
|                                   | decisions under Getting it Right  |
|                                   | (GIR).                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update the Claim Finalisation     |
|                                   | Note with the following, as       |
|                                   | relevant:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Discretionary decisions including |
|                                   | references to Operational         |
|                                   | Blueprint                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Names of any claimants removed    |
|                                   | from the claim and reason(s)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Document LGA claimed              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is ineligible,    |
|                                   | clearly document all reasons why, |
|                                   | including if they did not meet a  |
|                                   | valid impact reason, and/or if    |
|                                   | the customer did not claim a      |
|                                   | declared LGA (major damage impact |
|                                   | reasons only). Document all       |
|                                   | ineligible impact reason claimed  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is eligible,      |
|                                   | clearly document that the         |
|                                   | customer meets all eligibility    |
|                                   | criteria, and include the valid   |
|                                   | impact reason claimed             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Successful contact with customer  |
|                                   | to advise of unfavourable         |
|                                   | decisions:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Date and time contacted       |
|                                   |     customer                      |
|                                   | -   Information advised to        |
|                                   |     customer                      |
|                                   | -   Their review and appeal       |
|                                   |     rights                        |
|                                   | -   Unsuccessful contact with     |
|                                   |     customer to advise of         |
|                                   |     unfavourable decision:        |
|                                   | -   Contact attempt unsuccessful  |
|                                   | -   Contact: (record telephone    |
|                                   |     numbers used to attempt       |
|                                   |     contact; dates and times of   |
|                                   |     calls)                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer’s original claim    |
|                                   | was cancelled as they claimed the |
|                                   | incorrect event or payment        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer should have claimed |
|                                   | AGDRP instead of NZ DRP and was   |
|                                   | not eligible to claim for a       |
|                                   | dependent adult, spouse or child  |
|                                   | who lives with them (who is not   |
|                                   | their dependent child)            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If rejecting due to concerns      |
|                                   | about the validity of the claim,  |
|                                   | do not record the term ‘fraud’ on |
|                                   | the customer’s record. Depending  |
|                                   | on the reason, record:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If there are concerns about   |
|                                   |     validity of identity or       |
|                                   |     details in the claim          |
|                                   |     'The claim cannot be granted  |
|                                   |     due to concerns about the     |
|                                   |     validity of the details       |
|                                   |     provided, so eligibility      |
|                                   |     cannot be established’        |
|                                   | -   If the customer uploaded      |
|                                   |     false image/s:                |
|                                   |     'Image/s were found on the    |
|                                   |     internet and do not support   |
|                                   |     the customer’s claim for      |
|                                   |     major damage'                 |
|                                   | -   Tip-off form completed due to |
|                                   |     concerns about the validity   |
|                                   |     of the customer’s claim       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Finalise to complete the   |
|                                   | claim.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A confirmation dialog box will    |
|                                   | appear. Select OK.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a checklist of scans displays, |
|                                   | mark as complete using the tick   |
|                                   | boxes to close scans off the      |
|                                   | customer's record.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Claim needs to be allocated to a  |
|                                   | specialist team with keyword      |
|                                   | DRPSPEC                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | New South Wales Floods – July     |
|                                   | 2022 + Read more ...              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer is not eligible      |
|                                   | under a major damage impact       |
|                                   | reason but claims they have been  |
|                                   | impacted as a direct result of    |
|                                   | the disaster for at least one of  |
|                                   | the following reasons:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   seriously injured             |
|                                   | -   has a dependent child who has |
|                                   |     been seriously injured, or    |

|                                   |     member who has died or is     |
|                                   |     missing                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The claim is ineligible and does  |
|                                   | not have any of the following     |

|                                   | Officer to finalise the claim,    |

|                                   | needed.                           |

| 8                                 | E027FY error - customer contact   |
|                                   | was not successful + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This would have been identified   |

|                                   |     areas), select a date from    |
|                                   |     the calendar 36 days in the   |
|                                   |     future                        |

|                                   |     areas) select a date from the |
|                                   |     calendar 43 days in the       |
|                                   |     future                        |

|                                   |     selected                      |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |

|                                   | record. This will return to the   |

|                                   | Customer First. Note: staff       |

Customers without a confirmed identity status - ACC or paper claims only

Table 4: follow this process if when reviewing the claim the customer's
Identity Status does not show as Confirmed on the Transaction Summary
(TS) screen when reviewing the claim and the customer has lodged an ACC
or paper claim.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | ACC or paper claim + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if there are any concerns   |
|                                   | about the customer’s claim or     |
|                                   | identity, see Step 22 Table 1.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | At the Identity Status step in    |
|                                   | Table 1, if the customer does not |
|                                   | have an identity status of        |
|                                   | Confirmed, see Proof of identity  |
|                                   | (POI) for emergency payments.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Otherwise, continue processing    |
|                                   | the customer’s claim.             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Requesting evidence

Table 5: follow this process as directed in Table 1 or Table 2 above.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Try to contact the customer +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Before contacting a customer to   |
|                                   | ask for more information or       |
|                                   | evidence to support their claim,  |
|                                   | make sure:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   all pre-claim checks in Table |
|                                   |     1 and Table 2 have been       |
|                                   |     completed                     |
|                                   | -   the customer meets all other  |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria for      |
|                                   |     payment, and                  |
|                                   | -   all information needed from   |
|                                   |     the customer to support their |
|                                   |     claim is discussed in the one |
|                                   |     contact                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When requesting proof of          |
|                                   | identity, see Proof of identity   |
|                                   | (POI) requirements for emergency  |
|                                   | payments.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS) to the customer between     |
|                                   | 8:00 am and 8:00 pm using the     |
|                                   | customer's local time to let them |
|                                   | know a Service Officer will call  |
|                                   | them today from a private number. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer needs an      |
|                                   | interpreter, the 4 digit office   |
|                                   | code ID is 1897 for Smart Centre  |
|                                   | Emergency Management. See         |
|                                   | Contacting an on-demand telephone |
|                                   | interpreter (Interpreter          |
|                                   | Connect).                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the contact successful?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 2             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 4              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Contact successful - request      |
|                                   | evidence + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Evidence is only required in      |
|                                   | certain circumstances. Service    |
|                                   | Officers must refer to            |
|                                   | Definitions and evidence -        |
|                                   | adversely affected by a major     |
|                                   | disaster to determine if further  |
|                                   | evidence should be requested.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ask the customer to give Proof of |
|                                   | Record Ownership (PoRO). Do not   |
|                                   | give hints or prompts that help   |
|                                   | the customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   | questions                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Read the verbal request statement |
|                                   | for AGDRP/NZ DRP                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ask the customer to provide all   |
|                                   | required evidence to support      |
|                                   | their claim within 28 days        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note on the DL screen under the   |
|                                   | Document list/note section with   |
|                                   | the outcome of the discussion     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select Close document         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Encourage them to upload          |
|                                   | documents through the requested   |
|                                   | task in their online claim on the |
|                                   | day. This will allow their claim  |
|                                   | to be processed as soon as        |
|                                   | possible                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer agreed to the    |
|                                   | verbal request?                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 4              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Document verbal request for       |
|                                   | information + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer has agreed to a     |
|                                   | verbal request for information,   |
|                                   | annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | DL/Note: with the following       |
|                                   | details:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date verbal request was made:     |
|                                   | (insert date)                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The information is required to    |
|                                   | assess their entitlement for      |
|                                   | AGDRP or NZ DRP                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | What information is required:     |
|                                   | (insert full details)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reasonable Due Date: Add a date   |
|                                   | 28 days in the future. If contact |
|                                   | was unsuccessful, allow time to   |
|                                   | respond as per agency standards.  |
|                                   | For customers with:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar 30     |
|                                   |     days in the future            |
|                                   | -   no online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar, for   |
|                                   |     - metropolitan/regional       |
|                                   |     areas, 36 days in the future  |
|                                   |     - remote areas, 43 days in    |
|                                   |     the future                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | How they can get the information  |
|                                   | to the agency: (insert details,   |
|                                   | for example, using online         |
|                                   | account/upload documents, phone   |
|                                   | us, visit Service Centre/Agent or |
|                                   | via mail/fax)                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The following information was     |
|                                   | read to the customer: (Yes/No)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | 'The requested information (edit  |
|                                   | and insert details) is required   |
|                                   | to assess your eligibility for    |
|                                   | (insert details). This request    |
|                                   | has been made under Section 63 of |
|                                   | the Social Security               |
|                                   | Administration Act 1999. If you   |
|                                   | do not provide the requested      |
|                                   | information by (insert date),     |
|                                   | your (insert details, for         |
|                                   | example, claim may be rejected)'  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer acknowledged that they   |
|                                   | fully understood this request and |
|                                   | the consequence for not providing |
|                                   | the requested information:        |
|                                   | (Yes/No)                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Save.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   For all NZ DRP customers, or  |
|                                   |     if there are concerns an      |
|                                   |     AGDRP customer did not        |
|                                   |     understand the verbal         |
|                                   |     request, go to Step 4         |
|                                   | -   Otherwise, go to Step 5 to    |
|                                   |     place the claim on hold       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Send Request for Information      |
|                                   | (RFI) letter + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the information required from  |
|                                   | the customer can be provided      |
|                                   | verbally consider if sending a    |
|                                   | Q888 Request to contact letter    |
|                                   | will be sufficient. This letter   |
|                                   | advises the customer that we need |
|                                   | to speak to them to obtain        |
|                                   | details that will allow us to     |
|                                   | finalise their claim.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the Q888 Request to contact    |
|                                   | letter is sent                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note on the DL screen under the   |
|                                   | Document list/note section with   |
|                                   | the contact attempt details       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Include information that is       |
|                                   | required from the customer        |
|                                   | when/if they make contact         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select Close document         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Place the claim on hold for 14    |
|                                   | days                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here until the     |
|                                   | customer makes contact to discuss |
|                                   | or the hold expires. Then go to   |
|                                   | Step 6.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If physical evidence is needed.   |
|                                   | For example a form or photographs |
|                                   | to support major damage, an RFI   |
|                                   | letter must be sent:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   if evidence is needed to      |
|                                   |     assess eligibility for        |
|                                   |     payment as outlined in        |
|                                   |     Definitions and evidence -    |
|                                   |     adversely affected by a major |
|                                   |     disaster                      |
|                                   | -   when phone contact was not    |
|                                   |     successful                    |
|                                   | -   to an AGDRP customer who must |
|                                   |     give evidence and did not     |
|                                   |     agree to the verbal request,  |
|                                   |     or if there were any concerns |
|                                   |     they understood the request,  |
|                                   |     and                           |
|                                   | -   to all NZ DRP customers who   |
|                                   |     must give evidence, even if   |
|                                   |     they agreed to the verbal     |
|                                   |     request                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the customer’s claim select    |
|                                   | the More Options menu [more       |
|                                   | options] then Request Documents   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure all evidence required   |
|                                   | to support the customer’s claim   |
|                                   | is requested in the one letter.   |
|                                   | This will ensure a quicker        |
|                                   | outcome for the customer.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Benefit:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   AGDRP - select – AGP          |
|                                   |     -Disaster Recovery Payment    |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP - select – EXG         |
|                                   |     -Disaster Recovery Payments   |
|                                   |     for NZ non-protected SCV      |
|                                   |     (subclass 444)                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Authority to request:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   AGDRP claims - select –       |
|                                   |     Social Security               |
|                                   |     (Administration) Act 1999 –   |
|                                   |     Section 63                    |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP claims - select – None |
|                                   |     – Ex Gratia Payment use only  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Request: 1st                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer to contact: Call Centre  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Information to be supplied        |
|                                   | within: for customers with:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an online account, from the   |
|                                   |     drop down box select 28       |
|                                   |     days + Delivery               |
|                                   | -   no online account, from the   |
|                                   |     drop down box select ‘Other’  |
|                                   |     then select a date from the   |
|                                   |     calendar. For:                |
|                                   |     - metropolitan/regional       |
|                                   |     areas, 36 days in the future  |
|                                   |     - remote areas, 43 days in    |
|                                   |     the future. See Time allowed  |
|                                   |     to respond                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Search available documents |
|                                   | field, key 'DISASTER' to find     |
|                                   | related evidence for AGDRP/NZ DRP |
|                                   | claims, then select Search        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: evidence to request depends |
|                                   | on what staff have identified     |
|                                   | needs to be provided to finalise  |
|                                   | the customer’s claim. For help,   |
|                                   | contact Technical Peer Support.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Click on Select for all evidence  |
|                                   | required. When all evidence       |
|                                   | displays under Selected           |
|                                   | documents, select Next            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Generate print preview to  |
|                                   | review the letter                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Staff must review the letter  |
|                                   |     to check there are no errors  |
|                                   |     and it is easy to understand  |
|                                   | -   If the letter has any errors  |
|                                   |     and/or is not easy to         |
|                                   |     understand, staff must redo   |
|                                   |     it                            |
|                                   | -   To redo the letter, close the |
|                                   |     print preview                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close to exit the    |
|                                   |     letter                        |
|                                   |     - The Close Request box will  |
|                                   |     appear                        |
|                                   |     - Select OK                   |
|                                   |     - Go back to the More Options |
|                                   |     menu [more options] then      |
|                                   |     Request Documents to start    |
|                                   |     again. Note: any previously   |
|                                   |     saved options may need to be  |
|                                   |     removed if they were          |
|                                   |     incorrect.                    |
|                                   |     - Make the updates            |
|                                   |     - Select Generate print       |
|                                   |     preview to review the letter  |
|                                   |     again                         |
|                                   |     - If any more changes are     |
|                                   |     needed, redo the letter again |
|                                   |     as per the above steps        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Options: defaults to Print        |
|                                   | Central                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff notes: add information      |
|                                   | about the request or ‘Refer to    |
|                                   | Progress of Claim Note for the    |
|                                   | Claim ID (insert claim ID)’       |
|                                   |                                   |
