|                                   | Select Finalise to issue the      |
|                                   | letter                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 5                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | NZ DRP claims that need evidence  |
|                                   | of participation in the           |
|                                   | Australian Taxation system        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Search available documents |
|                                   | field, key PERSONAL TAX RETURN to |
|                                   | find related evidence for NZ DRP  |
|                                   | claims, then select Search        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Click on + Add                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the drop down, select the    |
|                                   | financial years evidence can be   |
|                                   | provided                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: one financial year at a     |
|                                   | time can be added. After adding   |
|                                   | one, repeat the above step to     |
|                                   | include the remaining 2 financial |
|                                   | years                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Click Save                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Click Next                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Generate print preview to  |
|                                   | review the letter                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Staff must review the letter  |
|                                   |     to check there are no errors  |
|                                   |     and it is easy to understand  |
|                                   | -   If the letter has any errors  |
|                                   |     and/or is not easy to         |
|                                   |     understand, staff must redo   |
|                                   |     it                            |
|                                   | -   To redo the letter, close the |
|                                   |     print preview                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close to exit the    |
|                                   |     letter                        |
|                                   |     - The Close Request box will  |
|                                   |     appear                        |
|                                   |     - Select OK                   |
|                                   |     - Go back to the More Options |
|                                   |     menu [more options] then      |
|                                   |     Request Documents to start    |
|                                   |     again. Note: any previously   |
|                                   |     saved options may need to be  |
|                                   |     removed if they were          |
|                                   |     incorrect.                    |
|                                   |     - Make the updates            |
|                                   |     - Select Generate print       |
|                                   |     preview to review the letter  |
|                                   |     again                         |
|                                   |     - If any more changes are     |
|                                   |     needed, redo the letter again |
|                                   |     as per the above steps        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Options: Print Central            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Request summary Final: include    |
|                                   | staff notes in text box provided  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Options: defaults to Print        |
|                                   | Central                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff notes: add information      |
|                                   | about the request or ‘Refer to    |
|                                   | Progress of Claim Note for the    |
|                                   | Claim ID (insert claim ID)’       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Finalise to issue the      |
|                                   | letter                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 5                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note + Read more ...              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claims pending POI:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Proof of identity (POI)       |
|                                   | requirements for emergency        |
|                                   | payments.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once the RFI is issued, Process   |
|                                   | Direct will update the claim      |
|                                   | status to ‘On hold’ with the      |
|                                   | relevant due date. Annotate the   |
|                                   | Progress of Claim Note on the DL  |
|                                   | screen under DL/Notes section.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Annotate                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Record details of why the claim   |
|                                   | is being placed on hold. For      |
|                                   | example:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim placed on hold pending  |
|                                   |     NRRA approval to reject       |
|                                   |     claims                        |
|                                   | -   Customer does not meet        |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria as       |
|                                   |     assets less than $20,000      |
|                                   | -   As at {date} customer does    |
|                                   |     not live in a declared area   |
|                                   | -   Customer has been requested   |
|                                   |     to provide evidence to        |
|                                   |     support claim e.g. evidence   |
|                                   |     of participation in           |
|                                   |     Australian Tax system for NZ  |
|                                   |     DRP                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not use the term ‘fraud’ if    |
|                                   | asking for evidence due to        |
|                                   | concerns about the validity of    |
|                                   | the customer’s claim              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an RFI was not sent, and the   |
|                                   | customer was advised to provide   |
|                                   | the requested evidence when       |
|                                   | submitting the claim, record      |
|                                   | conversation details in the Note  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Save                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Close document             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | It is important to record why the |
|                                   | claim is placed on hold. When the |
|                                   | hold period ends, the claim will  |
|                                   | return to the pool to be          |
|                                   | allocated for processing. The     |
|                                   | claim will be reassessed taking   |
|                                   | into account the details in the   |
|                                   | Progress of Claim Note on the DL  |
|                                   | screen under the Document         |
|                                   | list/note section.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here until         |
|                                   | requested evidence is provided or |
|                                   | the hold expires. Then go to Step |
|                                   | 6.                                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Evidence provided or hold         |
|                                   | expires + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Did the customer provide all      |
|                                   | required evidence or make contact |
|                                   | within the timeframe requested?   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, if the evidence means the    |
|                                   | customer                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   meets the eligibility         |
|                                   |     criteria                      |
|                                   |     -where evidence of an address |
|                                   |     change was requested as a     |
|                                   |     customer claimed a concurrent |
|                                   |     event, see Step 8 in Table 1  |
|                                   |     -otherwise, process the       |
|                                   |     claim, see Table 2            |
|                                   | -   does not meet the eligibility |
|                                   |     criteria, if approval has     |
|                                   |     -been given to reject claims, |
|                                   |     process the claim, see Table  |
|                                   |     2                             |
|                                   |     -not been given, place claim  |
|                                   |     on hold, see Step 2 in Table  |
|                                   |     3                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, if approval has               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   been given to reject claims,  |
|                                   |     process the claim, see Table  |
|                                   |     2                             |
|                                   | -   not been given, place claim   |
|                                   |     on hold, see Step 2 in Table  |
|                                   |     3                             |
|                                   |     -Note: if a claim was granted |
|                                   |     incorrectly (before evidence  |
|                                   |     was provided or the claim     |
|                                   |     hold expires) and the         |
|                                   |     customer should not have been |
|                                   |     paid, see Table 10            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Customer meets eligibility for a  |
|                                   | concurrent event + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer has provided        |
|                                   | evidence to support their claim   |
|                                   | for a concurrent event, the claim |
|                                   | cannot be processed. If staff try |
|                                   | to grant the claim, the following |
|                                   | error will display                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   E044FF - Event Prerequisite   |
|                                   |     not met                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must contact Technical Peer |
|                                   | Support who must                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   escalate the claim to the     |
|                                   |     Level 2 Helpdesk using the    |
|                                   |     payment query template, and   |
|                                   | -   place the claim on hold with  |
|                                   |     the reason Awaiting policy    |
|                                   |     advice. To put the claim on   |
|                                   |     hold, see Table 3 Step 2      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Claiming for children and secondary claimants after original claim granted

Table 6: follow this process as directed in Table 2 above to issue
payments for children or secondary claimants (for NZ DRP only) not
included in a claim already granted.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Customers contacts + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A new claim cannot be started     |
|                                   | when a:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | AGDRP/NZ DRP customer advises     |
|                                   | they                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   did not include a dependent   |
|                                   |     child/ren in their care in    |
|                                   |     their original claim          |
|                                   | -   did include a dependent       |
|                                   |     child/ren in their care in    |
|                                   |     their original claim and were |
|                                   |     not paid for that dependent   |
|                                   |     child/ren                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | NZ DRP customer advises they      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   did not include a secondary   |
|                                   |     claimant (partner, child      |
|                                   |     living with them who is not   |
|                                   |     their dependent child,        |
|                                   |     dependent adult) in their     |
|                                   |     original claim or             |
|                                   | -   did include a secondary       |
|                                   |     claimant (partner, child      |
|                                   |     living with them who is not   |
|                                   |     their dependent child,        |
|                                   |     dependent adult) in their     |
|                                   |     original claim and were not   |
|                                   |     paid for that secondary       |
|                                   |     claimant                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Locate the original claim to      |
|                                   | review the customer’s             |
|                                   | circumstances - this information  |
|                                   | will also need to be used when    |
|                                   | completing the new claim.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must decide if   |
|                                   | the customer is eligible for the  |
|                                   | additional payment/s, that is:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   for AGDRP and NZ DRP claiming |
|                                   |     for a dependent child/ren -   |
|                                   |     the child was under 16 and    |
|                                   |     not on an income support      |
|                                   |     payment on any day of the     |
|                                   |     event period. If not, tell    |
|                                   |     the customer the child will   |
|                                   |     need to make a claim on their |
|                                   |     own record                    |
|                                   | -   they are the principal carer  |
|                                   | -   a payment has not already     |
|                                   |     been paid for the child or    |
|                                   |     person being claimed          |
|                                   | -   for NZ DRP the secondary      |
|                                   |     claimant (including a child   |
|                                   |     who lives with them but who   |
|                                   |     is not a dependent child)     |
|                                   |     live at the same address      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer is claiming              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   AGDRP/NZ DRP for an           |
|                                   |     additional dependent          |
|                                   |     child/ren and may also be     |
|                                   |     claiming for a secondary      |
|                                   |     claimant/s. Dependent         |
|                                   |     child/ren details must be     |
|                                   |     checked as the customer must  |
|                                   |     be the principal carer of the |
|                                   |     child/ren Go to Step 2.       |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP for an additional      |
|                                   |     secondary claimant/s only     |
|                                   |     (including a child who lives  |
|                                   |     with them) and not for a      |
|                                   |     dependent child/ren, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 4                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | AGDRP/NZ DRP claim for additional |
|                                   | dependent children + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See the Is the customer claiming  |
|                                   | for a child/ren and               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is each dependent child linked to |
|                                   | the customer’s record steps of    |
|                                   | Table 1 when determining if a     |
|                                   | customer is the principal carer   |
|                                   | of a dependent child.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the customer recorded as the   |
|                                   | principal carer of the children   |
|                                   | being claimed?                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, go to Step 4                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, tell the customer our records |
|                                   | do not show they are the          |
|                                   | principal carer of the child. To  |
|                                   | be eligible for payment, they     |
|                                   | must be recorded as the principal |
|                                   | carer. Go to Step 3               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, for NZ DRP only does the      |
|                                   | customer want to claim for a      |
|                                   | child as a secondary claimant     |
|                                   | (not a dependent child)?          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 4             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 3              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | AGDRP/NZ DRP claim for additional |
|                                   | dependent children (cont.) + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | does want to proceed with         |
|                                   | claiming for the child, tell the  |
|                                   | customer a care assessment will   |
|                                   | need to be completed. Record the  |
|                                   | following in a Note:              |
|                                   | 'Summary: Care assessment         |
|                                   | required for AGDRP/NZ DRP         |
|                                   | Customer has advised they are the |
|                                   | principal carer of [name of       |
|                                   | child/ren].                       |
|                                   | Care assessment is needed to      |
|                                   | determine eligibility for         |
|                                   | AGDRP/NZ DRP to be paid to the    |
|                                   | customer for this child/ren.      |
|                                   | Customer has been advised to      |
|                                   | recontact after assessment        |
|                                   | completed, if principal carer     |
|                                   | status is confirmed. Customer     |
|                                   | transferred to the Families line  |
|                                   | '                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   tell the customer they will   |
|                                   |     need to recontact after their |
|                                   |     care assessment has been      |
|                                   |     finalised, and confirms they  |
|                                   |     are the principal carer       |
|                                   | -   transfer the customer to the  |
|                                   |     Families line                 |
|                                   | -   procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | does not want to proceed with the |
|                                   | claim, record details of the      |
|                                   | conversation in a Note (including |
|                                   | name of the child/ren). Procedure |
|                                   | ends here                         |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Check AGDRP/NZ DRP not already    |
|                                   | paid for a dependent child/ren or |
|                                   | secondary claimant/s + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Investigate the record to         |
|                                   | determine if AGDRP/NZ DRP has     |
|                                   | already been issued for the       |
|                                   | dependent child/ren Check         |
|                                   | AGDRP/NZ DRP not already paid for |
|                                   | a dependent child/ren or          |
|                                   | secondary claimant/s. The Claim   |
|                                   | Finalisation Note will record     |
|                                   | which dependent children and      |
|                                   | secondary claimants were paid     |
|                                   | when a claim is granted.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, contact Technical Peer  |
|                                   | Support.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has a payment already been issued |
|                                   | for all dependent child/ren and   |
|                                   | secondary claimant/s?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, and it has been determined   |
|                                   | the customer should               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   have received the payment for |
|                                   |     the dependent child/ren and   |
|                                   |     or secondary claimant(s).     |
|                                   |     Annotate the Progress of      |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document list/note  |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   |     Procedure ends here           |
|                                   | -   not have received payment,    |
|                                   |     including where the customer  |
|                                   |     should not have been paid as  |
|                                   |     they did not meet the         |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria, go to   |
|                                   |     Table 10                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 5                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | AGDRP/NZ DRP to be issued for a   |
|                                   | dependent child/ren and/or        |
|                                   | secondary claimant/s + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Open the Claim Summary from the   |
|                                   | original claim, as information    |
|                                   | will need to be included in the   |
|                                   | SOA shell.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the Process Direct home page |
|                                   | select SOA Shell:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Benefit Type for:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   AGDRP, select Disaster        |
|                                   |     Recovery Payment              |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP, select New Zealand    |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment - Ex-gratia  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Never select Emergency Payments   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer CRN: Enter customer’s    |
|                                   | CRN                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date of Receipt: Date customer    |
|                                   | contacted to claim for the        |
|                                   | child/ren and/or secondary        |
|                                   | claimant/s                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Create Claim.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Process.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Unselect all Task Selectors       |
|                                   | except for Disaster Recovery.     |
|                                   | Select Next.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete each screen in the       |
|                                   | Disaster Recovery workflow as per |
|                                   | the original Claim Summary:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure the correct answer      |
|                                   | about claiming for dependent      |
|                                   | children has been selected on the |
|                                   | Claim circumstance screen. If     |
|                                   | this is not selected, staff will  |
|                                   | not be presented with the         |
|                                   | Eligible Dependent Child(ren)     |
|                                   | Details screen to be able to      |
|                                   | include children in the           |
|                                   | assessment.                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Eligible Dependent         |
|                                   | Child(ren) Details screen, select |
|                                   | children to be paid               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure that link date for the  |
|                                   | child(ren) is before or the date  |
|                                   | of impact of the disaster         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If not, see the Child/ren not |
|                                   |     coded in care to cover date   |
|                                   |     of impact of the disaster     |
|                                   |     step in Table 1               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   New South Wales Floods –      |
|                                   |     February 2022, Go to Step 7   |
|                                   | -   all other emergency events,   |
|                                   |     go to Step 7                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Check if customer is eligible and |
|                                   | has already been paid the AGDRP   |
|                                   | (Special Supplement) for this     |
|                                   | event + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   customer’s details to find    |
|                                   |     out if they lived in an       |
|                                   |     eligible area at the time of  |
|                                   |     being impacted by the New     |
|                                   |     South Wales Floods - February |
|                                   |     2022 and were eligible to     |
|                                   |     receive the AGDRP (Special    |
|                                   |     Supplement)                   |
|                                   | -   DL screen under Notes for any |
|                                   |     Notes or DOCs on record that  |
|                                   |     confirm any payment of the    |
|                                   |     AGDRP (Special Supplement)    |
|                                   |     has already been made         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer been paid the    |
|                                   | AGDRP (Special Supplement) for    |
|                                   | the New South Wales Floods –      |
|                                   | February 2022?                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, the SOA claim for dependent  |
|                                   | child/ren and/or secondary        |
|                                   | claimant/s will not finalise      |
|                                   | without an error (E044FF )        |
|                                   | showing                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The SOA claim activity must   |
|                                   |     be left on the record         |
|                                   | -   Contact Technical Peer        |
|                                   |     Support who will escalate the |
|                                   |     claim to the Level 2 Helpdesk |
|                                   |     for finalisation using the    |
|                                   |     payment query template.       |
|                                   | -   Add a Note advising the       |
|                                   |     reason for escalation         |
|                                   | -   Place the claim on hold using |
|                                   |     the Hold Reason ‘System       |
|                                   |     Investigation’                |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 7                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Claiming for additional dependent |
|                                   | child/ren only?                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer is only claiming for an  |
|                                   | additional dependent child/ren    |
|                                   | only + Read more ...              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer is only claiming         |
|                                   | AGDRP/NZ DRP for an additional    |
|                                   | dependent child/ren only and not  |
|                                   | any secondary claimant/s, go to   |
|                                   | step 8.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer is claiming NZ DRP and   |
|                                   | this includes a secondary         |
|                                   | claimant + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: this may also include a     |
|                                   | dependent child/ren               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the staff member have access |
|                                   | to the !FFAP screen?              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, go to Step 8                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, do not finalise the claim     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Do not use the Handover to    |
|                                   |     CF/CR function                |
|                                   | -   To help the next Service      |
|                                   |     Officer who will finalise the |
|                                   |     claim, add all relevant       |
|                                   |     information in the Progress   |
|                                   |     of Claim Note on the DL       |
|                                   |     Screen under the Document     |
|                                   |     list/note section             |
|                                   | -   Add the keyword NOM to the    |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   |     - Select Keyword icon         |
|                                   |     - Select the Add button       |
|                                   |     - Key NOM in the keyword      |
|                                   |     search field (this keyword is |
|                                   |     to be used pending new        |
|                                   |     keyword for NZ DRP claims)    |
|                                   |     - Select the correct search   |
|                                   |     result to Save the keyword    |
|                                   | -   Go to the Inbox in Process    |
|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   | -   In Main Category select WLM   |
|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   |     - Select Multi-Select         |
|                                   |     - Select the transaction from |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   |     - Select Unassign at the      |
|                                   |     bottom of the screen to       |
|                                   |     unassign                      |
|                                   |     - Select the Reason of Second |
|                                   |     contact attempt required      |
|                                   |     - Select Submit               |
|                                   | -   The claim will be allocated   |
|                                   |     to a suitably trained Service |
|                                   |     Officer to finalise           |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Check if another Flexible Support |
|                                   | Payment (FSP) payment has been    |
|                                   | paid today + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the Payment Summary     |
|                                   |     (PS) screen by keying PS next |
|                                   |     to Super Key                  |
|                                   | -   Display payments for: select  |
|                                   |     FSP                           |
|                                   | -   Number of months in past: key |
|                                   |     4 months                      |
|                                   | -   Decide if any other FSP       |
|                                   |     payments have been paid on    |
|                                   |     the same day, for example,    |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has another FSP payment been paid |
|                                   | today?                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, 2 FSP payments cannot be     |
|                                   | released on the same day. Place   |
|                                   | the claim on hold                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Update Claim Status           |
|                                   | -   Select Status, change it to   |
|                                   |     On Hold and select Pending    |
|                                   |     Customer Contact. Note: this  |
|                                   |     is a system workaround and no |
|                                   |     customer contact is needed    |
|                                   | -   Change the On Hold Expiry     |
|                                   |     Date to 1 day in the future   |
|                                   |     (not 28 days)                 |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Annotate the Progress of      |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document list/note  |
|                                   |     section with details of why   |
|                                   |     the claim has been placed on  |
|                                   |     hold                          |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   If the claim is for NZ DRP    |
|                                   |     and includes a secondary      |
|                                   |     claimant add the keyword NOM  |
|                                   |     to the claim                  |
|                                   |     - Select Keyword icon         |
|                                   |     - Select the Add button       |
|                                   |     - Key NOM in the keyword      |
|                                   |     search field (this keyword is |
|                                   |     to be used pending new        |
|                                   |     keyword for NZ DRP claims)    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, and claim is for AGDRP/ NZ    |
|                                   | DRP and does not include a        |
|                                   | secondary claimants/(s go to Step |
|                                   | 9                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, and the claim is for NZ DRP   |
|                                   | and includes a secondary          |
|                                   | claimant/s, for to Step 10        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Claim Decision – claim has        |
|                                   | dependent child/ren only + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | As no secondary claimant/s are    |
|                                   | included in the claim, on the     |
|                                   | Claim Decision screen:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Grant outcome as per   |
|                                   |     original claim                |
|                                   | -   Include child payments only:  |
|                                   |     select Yes from the dropdown  |
|                                   |     menu                          |
|                                   | -   Payment Components: confirm   |
|                                   |     correct child payment         |
|                                   |     amount(s) display             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next and then select       |
|                                   | Assess to confirm the correct     |
|                                   | amount shows on the Entitlements  |
|                                   | (ELD) screen.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Finish to finalise the     |
|                                   | claim. Update the Claim           |
|                                   | Finalisation Note with any        |
|                                   | additional details needed. Select |
|                                   | Finalise.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 10                                | Claim includes secondary          |
|                                   | claimant/s + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This step must only be followed   |
|                                   | by staff with access to the !FFAP |
|                                   | screen who                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   are assessing a claim that    |
|                                   |     includes a secondary          |
|                                   |     claimant/s, or                |
|                                   | -   have been allocated a claim   |
|                                   |     with the NOM keyword that     |
|                                   |     includes a secondary          |
|                                   |     claimant/s.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: a dependent child/ren may   |
|                                   | also be included, not just a      |
|                                   | secondary claimant/s              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | As the claim includes secondary   |
|                                   | claimant/s handover to Customer   |
|                                   | First                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once the customer’s claim has     |
|                                   | been reviewed and a decision can  |
|                                   | be finalised, payment must be     |
|                                   | issued via !FFAP. Transfer the    |
|                                   | claim to Customer First.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select [more options] >       |
|                                   |     Handover to CF/CR             |
|                                   |     Do not select Handover to     |
|                                   |     CF/CR for any other reason    |
|                                   | -   On the Change Status screen,  |
|                                   |     select Reason: ‘FUA –         |
|                                   |     Function unavailable in PD’.  |
|                                   |     This will automatically place |
|                                   |     the claim in Process Direct   |
|                                   |     on hold indefinitely and      |
|                                   |     create a New Claim activity   |
|                                   |     in Customer First (for        |
|                                   |     example, AUS Gov Disaster     |
|                                   |     Recovery/New Claim with a     |
|                                   |     status of Started)            |
|                                   | -   Select the Home button at the |
|                                   |     top left hand side to exit    |
|                                   |     out of the transaction and    |
|                                   |     the customer’s record. This   |
|                                   |     will return to the Process    |
|                                   |     Direct landing page. Note:    |
|                                   |     staff should not have the     |
|                                   |     customer’s record open in     |
|                                   |     Customer First and Process    |
|                                   |     Direct at the same time, as   |
|                                   |     this can cause errors         |
|                                   | -   Go to the customer’s record   |
|                                   |     in Customer First             |
|                                   | -   Key AL in the Next field to   |
|                                   |     go to the Activity List (AL)  |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Select the New Claim          |
|                                   |     activity, and key !FFAP in    |
|                                   |     the Next field                |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 11                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 11                                | !FFAP screen in Customer First +  |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter details in the !FFAP screen |
|                                   | as per the details in the Claim   |
|                                   | Summary in Process Direct:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Event ID: To find this, see the   |
|                                   | Resources page in the Operational |
|                                   | Blueprint for the event           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Grant                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Grant reason: select from drop    |
|                                   | down                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date affected by event: key the   |
|                                   | date the customer was affected by |
|                                   | the major disaster                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the payment amount is       |
|                                   | correct                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the payment amount is to       |
|                                   | include a child:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Component Item ID: enter the      |
|                                   | child's CRN                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Add more children as needed, and  |
|                                   | key child’s CRN in Component Item |
|                                   | ID                                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the payment amount is to       |
|                                   | include a spouse or dependent     |
|                                   | adult:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Component Item ID: enter the  |
|                                   |     spouse or dependent adult’s   |
|                                   |     CRN                           |
|                                   | -   Add more dependent adults as  |
|                                   |     required, and enter the       |
|                                   |     dependent adult’s CRN in the  |
|                                   |     Component Item ID             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Source of the claim: key          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | PHO for phone claims              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | LET for paper claims              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter the Receipt date            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the Total Payable           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the payment destination    |
|                                   | with the code FSP in the Ben Type |
|                                   | Code column                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the payment destination   |
|                                   | details are correct or add        |
|                                   | details if needed                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Activity Notes add:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim handed over from PD as  |
|                                   |     secondary claimant/s added to |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   | -   Rate of payment. For example, |
|                                   |     LGA Noosa, 1 x Adult $1,000;  |
|                                   |     2 x Children $400 = $800;     |
|                                   |     TOTAL = $1,800                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Finalise the activity on the      |
|                                   | Assessments Results screen making |
|                                   | sure the outcome is correct       |
|                                   | before selecting Continue         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This will automatically change    |
|                                   | the status of the claim in        |
|                                   | Process Direct to Completed, but  |
|                                   | will not create a Claim           |
|                                   | Finalisation Note or Decision DOC |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete a mySupport form if      |
|                                   | there are system issues:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   stopping the payment, or      |
|                                   | -   incorrect payment amounts     |
|                                   |     show                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 12                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 12                                | Document decision in Customer     |
|                                   | First + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Finalising the claim via the  |
|                                   |     !FFAP screen auto-completes   |
|                                   |     the activity in Process       |
|                                   |     Direct. It does not create a  |
|                                   |     decision Claim Finalisation   |
|                                   |     Note in Process Direct or DOC |
|                                   |     in Customer First.            |
|                                   | -   Add a DOC to the customer’s   |
|                                   |     record in Customer First      |
|                                   |     using the Fast Note workflow: |
|                                   | -   Location: Customer First >    |
|                                   |     Workspace > Documents and     |
|                                   |     Correspondence > Fast Note -  |
|                                   |     Auto Text                     |
|                                   | -   Service Reason: select EXG -  |
|                                   |     Emergency Exgratia            |
|                                   | -   Document Completion: select   |
|                                   |     Yes, otherwise the Fast Note  |
|                                   |     will not close and creates a  |
|                                   |     new work item                 |
|                                   | -   Extra Details to enter a      |
|                                   |     title for the DOC. Type in    |
|                                   |     this field NZ DRP GRANTED     |
|                                   |     - Claim ID: <ID>              |
|                                   |     - Assessment date: <DD MMM    |
|                                   |     YYYY>                         |
|                                   |     - Event Name: <Disaster       |
|                                   |     name>_                        |
|                                   |     - Event Code: <Disaster code> |
|                                   |     - Grant Reason: <Reason text> |
|                                   |     - LGA claimed: <LGA name>     |
|                                   |     - Outcome: Grant              |
|                                   |     - Act reference: * NZ DRP,    |
|                                   |     granted under Section 32B of  |
|                                   |     the Financial Framework       |
|                                   |     (Supplementary Powers) Act    |
|                                   |     1997 created in these         |
|                                   |     circumstances.                |
|                                   |     - Note: all claim information |
|                                   |     is contained within the claim |
|                                   |     ID in Process Direct. For     |
|                                   |     more details, refer to this   |
|                                   |     claim.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
