Reporting potential fraud

Table 7

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Report suspected fraud + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff should Report suspected     |
|                                   | fraud If they:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   have concerns about the       |
|                                   |     identity of a person making a |
|                                   |     claim, or                     |
|                                   | -   suspect the customer is       |
|                                   |     acting fraudulently when      |
|                                   |     claiming AGDRP or NZ DRP      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Important points when reporting   |
|                                   | suspected fraud:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Do not investigate the record |
|                                   |     any further than is needed to |
|                                   |     complete regular duties       |
|                                   | -   Do not search the system for  |
|                                   |     customer information in order |
|                                   |     to complete the report        |
|                                   | -   Only provide details in the   |
|                                   |     report that were received or  |
|                                   |     became apparent during the    |
|                                   |     interaction with the customer |
|                                   |     or processing of the claim    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not grant the claim.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 2                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Record DOA DOC in Customer        |
|                                   | First + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will return to the   |
|                                   | Process Direct landing page.      |
|                                   | Pending DOA DOC functionality in  |
|                                   | Process Direct, access the        |
|                                   | customer’s record in Customer     |
|                                   | First to add a Display on Access  |
|                                   | (DOA) DOC. Any future claims      |
|                                   | lodged by the customer will not   |
|                                   | meet the rules for straight       |
|                                   | through processing.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: staff should not have the   |
|                                   | customer’s record open in         |
|                                   | Customer First and Process Direct |
|                                   | at the same time, as this can     |
|                                   | cause errors.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To create the DOA DOC in Customer |
|                                   | First run the Fast Note workflow: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Search Workspace: Key Fast     |
|                                   | Note then Select Search           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Fast Note hyperlink    |
|                                   | and complete the Fast Note        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Who contacted: From the drop down |
|                                   | box Select CSO Customer Service   |
|                                   | Officer                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Reason: From the drop     |
|                                   | down box select the following:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   For AGDRP, select AGP - AUS   |
|                                   |     Gov Disaster Recovery Payment |
|                                   | -   For NZDRP, select EXG -       |
|                                   |     Emergency Ex-gratia           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date of Receipt: Date DOC created |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Channel: From the drop down box   |
|                                   | select INT- Internal Channels     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Source: From the drop down select |
|                                   | INT-Internal                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Auto text. From the drop   |
|                                   | down box select:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Category 1: Emergency         |
|                                   | -   Category 2: Claim             |
|                                   | -   Template: Caution for         |
|                                   |     Emergency Pymts               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Display on Access          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Confirm                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DOA reason screen                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reason: Auto populates to SCC –   |
|                                   | Special Contact Considerations    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Expiry Date: auto populates   |
|                                   | -   Select Confirm                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Answer all questions and prompts  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For DOA DOC about false image/s   |
|                                   | uploaded, include:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim for AGDRP/NZ DRP should |
|                                   |     not be granted for this       |
|                                   |     customer for {INSERT EVENT    |
|                                   |     NAME}                         |
|                                   |     If the customer contacts      |
|                                   |     about the status of their     |
|                                   |     claim they can be advised:    |
|                                   |     'the image uploaded has been  |
|                                   |     found using an internet image |
|                                   |     search and does not support   |
|                                   |     your claim for major damage,  |
|                                   |     so your claim cannot be       |
|                                   |     granted as eligibility cannot |
|                                   |     be established'               |
|                                   |     False image/s has/have been   |
|                                   |     reported                      |
|                                   |     Delete as appropriate         |
|                                   |     Claim is on hold pending      |
|                                   |     formal approval to reject     |
|                                   |     claims for this event         |
|                                   |     Claim has been rejected as    |
|                                   |     formal approval has been      |
|                                   |     given to reject claims for    |
|                                   |     this event                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For DOA DOC about identity or     |
|                                   | claim details, include:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim for AGDRP/NZ DRP should |
|                                   |     not be granted for this       |
|                                   |     customer for {INSERT EVENT    |
|                                   |     NAME} unless documentary      |
|                                   |     evidence is provided          |
|                                   |     If the customer contacts      |
|                                   |     about the status of their     |
|                                   |     claim they can be advised:    |
|                                   |     Delete as appropriate         |
|                                   |     Customer’s identity could not |
|                                   |     be confirmed. Additional      |
|                                   |     proof of identity documents   |
|                                   |     must be provided for your     |
|                                   |     claim to be assessed, or your |
|                                   |     claim cannot be granted, as   |
|                                   |     identity cannot be            |
|                                   |     established.                  |
|                                   |     Customer’s circumstances of   |
|                                   |     adverse impact cannot be      |
|                                   |     confirmed. Evidence to        |
|                                   |     support the adverse impact    |
|                                   |     claimed must be provided for  |
|                                   |     your claim to be assessed, or |
|                                   |     your claim cannot be granted, |
|                                   |     as eligibility cannot be      |
|                                   |     established.                  |
|                                   |     Delete as appropriate         |
|                                   |     Claim is on hold pending      |
|                                   |     formal approval to reject     |
|                                   |     claims for this event         |
|                                   |     Claim has been rejected as    |
|                                   |     formal approval has been      |
|                                   |     given to reject claims for    |
|                                   |     this event                    |
|                                   |     Delete as appropriate         |
|                                   |     Validity of customer’s        |
|                                   |     identity / claims made by the |
|                                   |     customer has been referred    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not use the term ‘fraud’ in    |
|                                   | the DOA DOC or if speaking with a |
|                                   | customer.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 3.                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Annotate the Note in Process      |
|                                   | Direct + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Close the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Customer First. Return to the     |
|                                   | customer’s claim in Process       |
|                                   | Direct.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note on the DL screen under the   |
|                                   | Document list/note section:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Annotate               |

|                                   |     Refer to DOA DOC dated        |
|                                   |     (insert date)'                |

|                                   | -   Select Close document         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The claim should be rejected. If  |

|                                   |                                   |
