!FFAP screen - processing claims

Table 8: how to finalise claims when there is a payment nominee or NZ
DRP claims with dependent adult/child claims (where child lives with the
customer (not a dependent child), spouse, and/or dependent adult. For
when to use this table, see Primary claimant claims for secondary
claimant in Eligibility for AGDRP and NZ DRP.

Staff must not follow this process unless assigned one of the above
claim types and have the required access to !FFAP screen.
Only staff with access to Flexible Support Payment FFAP can finalise
these claims in Customer First.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | AGDRP and NZ DRP claims to be     |
|                                   | finalised in Customer First +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Pending system updates, if:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | AGDRP or NZ DRP is to be issued   |
|                                   | to a payment nominee and the      |
|                                   | X032AS - No Payment Destination,  |
|                                   | please update via PA screen error |
|                                   | shows in Process Direct stopping  |
|                                   | the claim from finalising (that   |
|                                   | is, the customer has not          |
|                                   | previously claimed an FSP         |
|                                   | payment), or                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | NZ DRP is to be paid for a        |
|                                   | secondary claimant (that is,      |
|                                   | partner, dependent adult or child |
|                                   | living with the customer)         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the dependent                 |
|                                   |     partner/adult/child does not  |
|                                   |     need to be linked to the      |
|                                   |     customer's record - their CRN |
|                                   |     will be entered into the      |
|                                   |     !FFAP workflow for payment    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The payments must be issued in    |
|                                   | Customer First using the !FFAP    |
|                                   | screen. Only staff with access to |
|                                   | FSPFFAP resource can action these |
|                                   | claims.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The system will allocate the      |
|                                   | claim to an appropriately trained |
|                                   | Service Officer with !FFAP access |
|                                   | to finalise the claim, when:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the customer has a nominee    |
|                                   |     arrangement and the X032AS -  |
|                                   |     No Payment Destination,       |
|                                   |     please update via PA screen   |
|                                   |     error shows in Process Direct |
|                                   |     stopping the claim from       |
|                                   |     finalising (that is, the      |
|                                   |     customer has not previously   |
|                                   |     claimed an FSP payment), and  |
|                                   | -   the keyword NOM has been      |
|                                   |     applied to the claim          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These staff will be able to issue |
|                                   | any payments and finalise the     |
|                                   | claim outside Process Direct.     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Access + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the staff member have access |
|                                   | to !FFAP screen?                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, go to Step 3                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, do not action. If staff       |
|                                   | without !FFAP access have been    |
|                                   | assigned a claim which, during    |
|                                   | assessment, is identified as:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Payment having to be made to  |
|                                   |     a payment nominee, or         |
|                                   | -   An NZ DRP claim with          |
|                                   |     secondary claimants (that is, |
|                                   |     spouse, dependent adult or    |
|                                   |     non-dependent child living    |
|                                   |     with them)                    |
|                                   |     The payments need to be       |
|                                   |     issued and the claim          |
|                                   |     finalised in Customer First:  |
|                                   | -   Do not use the Handover to    |
|                                   |     CF/CR function                |
|                                   | -   To help the next Service      |
|                                   |     officer, Annotate the         |
|                                   |     Progress of Claim Note on the |
|                                   |     DL screen under the Document  |
|                                   |     list/note section with any    |
|                                   |     relevant information already  |
|                                   |     obtained or assessed          |
|                                   |     - Select Save                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close document       |
|                                   | -   Add the keyword NOM to the    |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   |     - Select Keyword icon         |
|                                   |     - Select the Add button       |
|                                   |     - Key NOM in the keyword      |
|                                   |     search field (this keyword is |
|                                   |     to be used pending new        |
|                                   |     keyword for NZ DRP claims)    |
|                                   |     - Select the correct search   |
|                                   |     result which will Save the    |
|                                   |     keyword                       |
|                                   | -   Go to the Inbox in Process    |
|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   | -   In Main Category select WLM   |
|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   |     - Select Multi-Select         |
|                                   |     - Select the transaction from |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   |     - Select Unassign at the      |
|                                   |     bottom of the screen to       |
|                                   |     unassign                      |
|                                   |     - Select the Reason of Second |
|                                   |     contact attempt required      |
|                                   |     - Select Submit               |
|                                   | -   The claim will be allocated   |
|                                   |     to a suitably trained Service |
|                                   |     Officer to make the           |
|                                   |     assessment                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Review the claim + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete the claim pre-checks and |
|                                   | process the claim using the steps |
|                                   | above to determine if the         |
|                                   | customer is eligible to receive a |
|                                   | payment. See the Progress of      |
|                                   | Claim Note on the DL screen under |
|                                   | the Document list/note section    |
|                                   | for any information recorded by   |
|                                   | the previous Service Officer (if  |
|                                   | applicable).                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the customer eligible for      |
|                                   | payment?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, go to Step 4                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, the claim should be rejected. |
|                                   | If approval has:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   been given to reject claims:  |
|                                   |     - For NZ DRP claims without a |
|                                   |     payment nominee, see Table 2  |
|                                   |     to process the claim          |
|                                   |     - For claims with a payment   |
|                                   |     nominee, go to Step 4         |
|                                   | -   not been given, see Step 1 in |
|                                   |     Table 3                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Handover to Customer First + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once the customer’s claim has     |
|                                   | been reviewed and a decision can  |
|                                   | be finalised (to grant or         |
|                                   | reject), check to make sure the   |
|                                   | claim needs to be finalised in    |
|                                   | the !FFAP screen.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has previously    |
|                                   | claimed an FSP payment and this   |
|                                   | shows on the Payment Destination  |
|                                   | Details (PAS) screen, the:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   X032AS – No Payment           |
|                                   |     Destination, please update    |
|                                   |     via PA screen error should    |
|                                   |     not show, and                 |
|                                   | -   claim should be processed in  |
|                                   |     Process Direct                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim does not need to be  |
|                                   | processed in the !FFAP screen, go |
|                                   | to Table 2.                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Otherwise transfer the claim to   |
|                                   | Customer First.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select [more options] >       |
|                                   |     Handover to CF/CR             |
|                                   |     Do not select Handover to     |
|                                   |     CF/CR for any other reason    |
|                                   | -   On the Change Status screen,  |
|                                   |     select Reason: ‘FUA –         |
|                                   |     Function unavailable in PD’.  |
|                                   |     This will automatically place |
|                                   |     the claim in Process Direct   |
|                                   |     on hold indefinitely and      |
|                                   |     create a New Claim activity   |
|                                   |     in Customer First (for        |
|                                   |     example, AUS Gov Disaster     |
|                                   |     Recovery/New Claim with a     |
|                                   |     status of Started)            |
|                                   | -   Select the Home button at the |
|                                   |     top left hand side to exit    |
|                                   |     out of the transaction and    |
|                                   |     the customer’s record. This   |
|                                   |     will return to the Process    |
|                                   |     Direct landing page. Note:    |
|                                   |     staff should not have the     |
|                                   |     customer’s record open in     |
|                                   |     Customer First and Process    |
|                                   |     Direct at the same time, as   |
|                                   |     this can cause errors         |
|                                   | -   Go to the customer’s record   |
|                                   |     in Customer First             |
|                                   | -   Key AL in the Next field to   |
|                                   |     go to the Activity List (AL)  |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Select the New Claim          |
|                                   |     activity, and key !FFAP in    |
|                                   |     the Next field                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the claim to be granted?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 5             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 6              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | !FFAP screen in Customer First -  |
|                                   | granted claims + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This process applies to claims    |
|                                   | with a payment nominee where the  |
|                                   | X032AS - No Payment Destination,  |
|                                   | please update via PA screen error |
|                                   | shows in Process Direct stopping  |
|                                   | the claim from finalising (that   |
|                                   | is, the customer has not          |
|                                   | previously claimed an FSP         |
|                                   | payment) and NZ DRP secondary     |
|                                   | claimant claims.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter details in the !FFAP screen |
|                                   | as per the details in the Claim   |
|                                   | Summary in Process Direct or      |
|                                   | paper claim:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Event ID: To find this, see the   |
|                                   | Resources page in the Operational |
|                                   | Blueprint for the event           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Grant                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Grant reason: select from drop    |
|                                   | down                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date affected by event: key the   |
|                                   | date the customer was affected by |
|                                   | the major disaster                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the payment amount is       |
|                                   | correct                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the payment amount is to       |
|                                   | include a child:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Component Item ID: enter the  |
|                                   |     child's CRN                   |
|                                   | -   Add more children as needed,  |
|                                   |     and key child’s CRN in        |
|                                   |     Component Item ID             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the payment amount is to       |
|                                   | include a spouse or dependent     |
|                                   | adult:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Component Item ID: enter the  |
|                                   |     spouse or dependent adult’s   |
|                                   |     CRN                           |
|                                   | -   Add more dependent adults as  |
|                                   |     required, and enter the       |
|                                   |     dependent adult’s CRN in the  |
|                                   |     Component Item ID             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Source of the claim: key          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   PHO for phone claims          |
|                                   | -   LET for paper claims          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter the Receipt date            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the Total Payable           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the payment destination    |
|                                   | with the code FSP in the Ben Type |
|                                   | Code column                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the payment destination   |
|                                   | details are correct or add        |
|                                   | details if needed                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Activity Notes add:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim handed over from PD     |
|                                   | -   Rate of payment. For example, |
|                                   |     LGA Noosa, 1 x Adult $1,000;  |
|                                   |     2 x Children $400 = $800;     |
|                                   |     TOTAL = $1,800                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Finalise the activity on the      |
|                                   | Assessments Results screen making |
|                                   | sure the outcome is correct       |
|                                   | before selecting Continue         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This will automatically change    |
|                                   | the status of the claim in        |
|                                   | Process Direct to Completed, but  |
|                                   | will not create a Claim           |
|                                   | Finalisation Note or Decision DOC |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete a mySupport form if      |
|                                   | there are system issues:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   stopping the payment, or      |
|                                   | -   incorrect payment amounts     |
|                                   |     show                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 7.                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | !FFAP screen in Customer First -  |
|                                   | rejected claims + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This process applies to claims    |
|                                   | with a payment nominee, the       |
|                                   | X032AS - No Payment Destination,  |
|                                   | please update via PA screen error |
|                                   | shows in Process Direct stopping  |
|                                   | the claim from finalising (that   |
|                                   | is, the customer has not          |
|                                   | previously claimed an FSP         |
|                                   | payment), which are to be         |
|                                   | rejected.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter details in the !FFAP screen |
|                                   | as per the details in the Claim   |
|                                   | Summary in Process Direct or      |
|                                   | paper claim:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter the Event ID                |
|                                   | To find the Event ID, see the     |
|                                   | Resources page in the Operational |
|                                   | Blueprint for the event           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Reject                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the drop down, select the    |
|                                   | Reject reason                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter the Source of the claim as: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   WEB for online claims         |
|                                   | -   PHO for phone claims          |
|                                   | -   LET for paper claims          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter the Receipt date            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue on the next 2     |
|                                   | screens                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Note: the system will not     |
|                                   |     allow the details of a child, |
|                                   |     spouse or dependent adult to  |
|                                   |     be added when rejecting the   |
|                                   |     claim on the !FFAP screen     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Activity Notes add:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim handed over from PD –   |
|                                   |     refer to DOC                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Finalise the activity on the      |
|                                   | Assessments Results screen making |
|                                   | sure the outcome is correct       |
|                                   | before selecting Continue         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This will automatically change    |
|                                   | the status of the claim in        |
|                                   | Process Direct to Completed, but  |
|                                   | will not create a Claim           |
|                                   | Finalisation Note or Decision DOC |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Document decision in Customer     |
|                                   | First + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Granted claims                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Finalising the claim via the      |
|                                   | !FFAP screen auto-completes the   |
|                                   | activity in Process Direct. It    |
|                                   | does not create a decision Claim  |
|                                   | Finalisation Note in Process      |
|                                   | Direct or DOC in Customer First.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Add a DOC to the customer’s       |
|                                   | record in Customer First using    |
|                                   | the Fast Note workflow:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Location: Customer First >    |
|                                   |     Workspace > Documents and     |
|                                   |     Correspondence > Fast Note -  |
|                                   |     Auto Text                     |
|                                   | -   Service Reason: select AGP –  |
|                                   |     AUS Gov Disaster Recovery     |
|                                   |     (for AGDRP) or EXG -          |
|                                   |     Emergency Exgratia (for NZ    |
|                                   |     DRP) as appropriate           |
|                                   | -   Document Completion: select   |
|                                   |     Yes, otherwise the Fast Note  |
|                                   |     will not close and creates a  |
|                                   |     new work item                 |
|                                   | -   Extra Details to enter a      |
|                                   |     title for the DOC. Type in    |
|                                   |     this field *AGDRP/NZ DRP      |
|                                   |     GRANTED or *AGDRP/NZ DRP      |
|                                   |     REJECTED (*delete as          |
|                                   |     appropriate)                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | AGDRP /NZ DRP granted:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Claim ID: <ID>                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Assessment date: <DD MMM YYYY>  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Event Name: <Disaster name>     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Event Code: <Disaster code>     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Grant Reason: <Reason text>     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - LGA claimed: <LGA name>         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Outcome: Grant                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Act reference: * AGDRP, granted |
|                                   | under Section 1061K of the Social |
|                                   | Security Act 1991                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | * NZ DRP, granted under Section   |
|                                   | 32B of the Financial Framework    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | (Supplementary Powers) Act 1997   |
|                                   | created in these circumstances.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Note: all claim information is  |
|                                   | contained within the claim ID in  |
|                                   | Process Direct. For more details, |
|                                   | refer to this claim.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | * Delete as appropriate           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Rejected claims                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Finalising the claim via the      |
|                                   | !FFAP screen auto-completes the   |
|                                   | activity in Process Direct. It    |
|                                   | does not create a decision Claim  |
|                                   | Finalisation Note in Process      |
|                                   | Direct or DOC in Customer First.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Add a DOC to the customer’s       |
|                                   | record in Customer First using    |
|                                   | the Fast Note workflow:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Location: Customer First >        |
|                                   | Workspace > Documents and         |
|                                   | Correspondence > Fast Note - Auto |
|                                   | Text                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Reason: select AGP – AUS  |
|                                   | Gov Disaster Recovery (for AGDRP) |
|                                   | or EXG - Emergency Exgratia (for  |
|                                   | NZ DRP) as appropriate            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Document Completion: select Yes,  |
|                                   | otherwise the Fast Note will not  |
|                                   | close and creates a new work item |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Extra Details to enter a title    |
|                                   | for the DOC. Type in this field   |
|                                   | *AGDRP/NZ DRP REJECTED (*Delete   |
|                                   | as appropriate)                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | AGDRP / NZ DRP rejected:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Claim ID: <ID>                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Assessment date: <DD MMM YYYY>  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Event Name: <Disaster name>     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Event Code: <Disaster code>     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Outcome: Reject                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - LGA claimed: <LGA name>         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Rejection reason: (include if   |
|                                   | the customer claimed a major      |
|                                   | damage impact reason and did not  |
|                                   | claim a declared LGA)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Act reference: * AGDRP,         |
|                                   | rejected under Section 1061K of   |
|                                   | the Social Security Act 1991      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | * NZ DRP, rejected under Section  |
|                                   | 32B of the Financial Framework    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | (Supplementary Powers) Act 1997   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Customer has been contacted to  |
|                                   | advise of the rejection reason?   |
|                                   | Yes/No                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Appeal rights provided to the   |
|                                   | customer? * Yes/No                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Note: all claim information is  |
|                                   | contained within the claim ID in  |
|                                   | Process Direct. For more details, |
|                                   | refer to this claim.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | * Delete as appropriate           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | AGDRP / NZ DRP rejected as        |
|                                   | evidence not provided:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Claim ID: <ID>                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Assessment date: <DD MMM YYYY>  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Event Name: <Disaster name>     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Event Code: <Disaster code>     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Grant Reason: <Reason text>     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Outcome: Reject                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Failed to reply to request for  |
|                                   | further information/evidence      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Act reference: * AGDRP,         |
|                                   | rejected under Section 1061K of   |
|                                   | the Social Security Act 1991      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | * NZ DRP, rejected under Section  |
|                                   | 32B of the Financial Framework    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | (Supplementary Powers) Act 1997   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | - Note: all claim information is  |
|                                   | contained within the claim ID in  |
|                                   | Process Direct. For more details, |
|                                   | refer to this claim.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | * Delete as appropriate           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Annotate Progress of Claim        |
|                                   | DL/Note in Process Direct + Read  |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After finalising the activity on  |
|                                   | the !FFAP screen in Customer      |
|                                   | First, the claim status in        |
|                                   | Process Direct will update to     |
|                                   | Completed.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update the Progress of Claim      |
|                                   | DL/Note:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Annotate button    |
|                                   | -   Add the following 'Payment    |
|                                   |     issued via !FFAP in CF' or    |
|                                   |     'Payment rejected in CF’ as   |
|                                   |     appropriate                   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Customer has been paid the incorrect payment

Table 9: Process to follow when:

-   AGDRP was paid when NZ DRP should have been paid, or
-   NZ DRP was paid and AGDRP should have been paid

If a payment has been issued incorrectly and the payment was made by NPP
or immediate payment this cannot be stopped by the Stop Payment process
with help from the ICT Service Desk. Do not follow steps in Payment of
arrears after reassessment.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | AGDRP or NZ DRP should have been  |
|                                   | paid instead + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP was paid when AGDRP    |
|                                   |     should have been, go to Step  |
|                                   |     2                             |
|                                   | -   AGDRP was paid when NZ DRP    |
|                                   |     should have been, go to Step  |
|                                   |     3                             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Was NZ DRP paid when AGDRP should |
|                                   | have been? + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the customer’s record to   |
|                                   | make sure the customer should     |
|                                   | have been paid AGDRP. See         |
|                                   | Eligibility for AGDRP and NZ DRP. |
|                                   | For help, contact Technical Peer  |
|                                   | Support.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has been granted  |
|                                   | NZ DRP when AGDRP was the correct |
|                                   | payment, has eligibility for      |
|                                   | AGDRP been established?           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, payment was correctly        |
|                                   | granted:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Annotate the AGDRP/NZDRP      |
|                                   |     Claim- Grant Summary Note by  |
|                                   |     selecting the Annotate        |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Record the reason why the     |
|                                   |     claim was correctly granted   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, see Table 10                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Was AGDRP paid when NZ DRP should |
|                                   | have been? + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the customer’s record to   |
|                                   | make sure the customer should     |
|                                   | have been paid NZ DRP. See        |
|                                   | Eligibility for AGDRP and NZ DRP. |
|                                   | For help, contact Technical Peer  |
|                                   | Support.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer met the          |
|                                   | ‘participated in the Australian   |
|                                   | tax system’ requirement and       |
|                                   | provided the required evidence?   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Annotate the AGDRP/NZDRP      |
|                                   |     Claim- Grant Summary Note by  |
|                                   |     selecting the Annotate        |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Record the reason why the     |
|                                   |     claim was correctly granted   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 4                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Customer should have claimed NZ   |
|                                   | DRP - evidence of participation   |
|                                   | in the Australian tax system is   |
|                                   | needed                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For surge capability staff not    |
|                                   | able to make outbound calls +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Contact Technical Peer        |
|                                   |     Support                       |
|                                   | -   They must escalate the claim  |
|                                   |     to the Level 2 Helpdesk using |
|                                   |     the payment query template    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For staff who can make outbound   |
|                                   | calls + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS) to the customer between     |
|                                   | 8:00 am and 8:00 pm using the     |
|                                   | customer's local time to let them |
|                                   | know a Service Officer will call  |
|                                   | them today from a private number. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer needs an      |
|                                   | interpreter, the 4 digit office   |
|                                   | code ID is 1897 for Smart Centre  |
|                                   | Emergency Management. See         |
|                                   | Contacting an on-demand telephone |
|                                   | interpreter (Interpreter          |
|                                   | Connect).                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the contact successful?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 5             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 7              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Contact successful - request      |
|                                   | evidence + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Ask the customer to give      |
|                                   |     Proof of Record Ownership     |
|                                   |     (PoRO). Do not give hints or  |
|                                   |     prompts that help the         |
|                                   |     customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   |     questions                     |
|                                   | -   Read the verbal request       |
|                                   |     statement for AGDRP/NZ DRP    |
|                                   | -   Ask the customer to provide   |
|                                   |     the required evidence of      |
|                                   |     participation in the          |
|                                   |     Australian tax system within  |
|                                   |     28 days                       |
|                                   | -   Record the outcome of the     |
|                                   |     discussion by annotating the  |
|                                   |     AGDRP/NZDRP Claim- Grant      |
|                                   |     Summary Note                  |
|                                   | -   Encourage them to upload      |
|                                   |     documents through the         |
|                                   |     requested task in their       |
|                                   |     online claim on the day. This |
|                                   |     will allow their claim to be  |
|                                   |     processed as soon as possible |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer agreed to the    |
|                                   | verbal request?                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 6             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 7              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Document verbal request for       |
|                                   | information + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer has agreed to a     |
|                                   | verbal request for information,   |
|                                   | annotate the AGDRP/NZDRP Claim-   |
|                                   | Grant Summary Note with the       |
|                                   | following details:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date verbal request was made:     |
|                                   | (insert date)                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The information is required to    |
|                                   | determine whether the customer    |
|                                   | was eligible for NZ DRP           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | What information is required:     |
|                                   | (insert full details)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reasonable Due Date: Add a date   |
|                                   | 28 days in the future. If contact |
|                                   | was unsuccessful, allow time to   |
|                                   | respond as per agency standards.  |
|                                   | For customers with:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar 30     |
|                                   |     days in the future            |
|                                   | -   no online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar, for   |
|                                   |     - metropolitan/regional       |
|                                   |     areas, 36 days in the future  |
|                                   |     - remote areas, 43 days in    |
|                                   |     the future                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | How they can get the information  |
|                                   | to the agency: (insert details,   |
|                                   | for example, using online         |
|                                   | account/upload documents, phone   |
|                                   | us, visit Service Centre/Agent or |
|                                   | via mail/fax)                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The following information was     |
|                                   | read to the customer: (Yes/No)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | 'The requested information (edit  |
|                                   | and insert details) is required   |
|                                   | to assess your eligibility for NZ |
|                                   | DRP. This request has been made   |
|                                   | under Section 63 of the Social    |
|                                   | Security Administration Act 1999. |
|                                   | If you do not provide the         |
|                                   | requested information by (insert  |
|                                   | date), your (insert details, for  |
|                                   | example, claim may be rejected)'  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer acknowledged that they   |
|                                   | fully understood this request and |
|                                   | the consequence for not providing |
|                                   | the requested information:        |
|                                   | (Yes/No)                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Save                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 7                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Send Request for Information      |
|                                   | (RFI) letter + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the customer record in Process |
|                                   | Direct, select the More Options   |
|                                   | menu [more options] then Request  |
|                                   | Documents to send a Request for   |
|                                   | Information (RFI) letter.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure all evidence required   |
|                                   | to support the customer’s claim   |
|                                   | is requested in the one letter.   |
|                                   | This will ensure a quicker        |
|                                   | outcome for the customer.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Benefit:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP - select - Disaster    |
|                                   |     Recovery Payments for NZ      |
|                                   |     non-protected SCV (subclass   |
|                                   |     444)                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Request: 1st                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer to contact: Call Centre  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Information to be supplied        |
|                                   | within: from the dropdown, select |
|                                   | 28 days                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the search field, key          |
|                                   | 'DISASTER' to find related        |
|                                   | evidence for AGDRP/NZ DRP claims, |
|                                   | then select Search                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Click on Select for all evidence  |
|                                   | required. One all evidence        |
|                                   | displays under Selected           |
|                                   | documents, select Next            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Generate print preview to  |
|                                   | review the letter                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Staff must review the letter  |
|                                   |     to check there are no errors  |
|                                   |     and it is easy to understand  |
|                                   | -   If the letter has any errors  |
|                                   |     and/or is not easy to         |
|                                   |     understand, staff must redo   |
|                                   |     it                            |
|                                   | -   To redo the letter, close the |
|                                   |     print preview                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close to exit the    |
|                                   |     letter                        |
|                                   |     - The Close Request box will  |
|                                   |     appear                        |
|                                   |     - Select OK                   |
|                                   |     - Go back to the More Options |
|                                   |     menu [more options] then      |
|                                   |     Request Documents to start    |
|                                   |     again. Note: any previously   |
|                                   |     saved options may need to be  |
|                                   |     removed if they were          |
|                                   |     incorrect.                    |
|                                   |     - Make the updates            |
|                                   |     - Select Generate print       |
|                                   |     preview to review the letter  |
|                                   |     again                         |
|                                   |     - If any more changes are     |
|                                   |     needed, redo the letter again |
|                                   |     as per the above steps        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Options: defaults to Print        |
|                                   | Central                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff notes: add information      |
|                                   | about the request or Refer to     |
|                                   | Progress of Claim Note for the    |
|                                   | Claim ID (insert claim ID)        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Finalise to issue the      |
|                                   | letter                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 8                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Add a manual review in Customer   |
|                                   | First + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Customer First                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Note: staff should not have   |
|                                   |     the customer’s record open in |
|                                   |     Customer First and Process    |
|                                   |     Direct at the same time, as   |
|                                   |     this can cause errors         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Code a manual review on the       |
|                                   | Review Registration (RVR) screen: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Reason: select EMG    |
|                                   | -   Review Reason: select Return  |
|                                   |     of Correspondence             |
|                                   | -   Due date: key ‘+ 36’          |
|                                   | -   Source: select an appropriate |
|                                   |     option. Note: the option      |
|                                   |     selected will not impact the  |
|                                   |     manual review                 |
|                                   | -   Date of Receipt: today’s date |
|                                   |     (date letter is sent)         |
|                                   | -   Keyword: EVD                  |
|                                   | -   Transfer to region: key ‘EPT’ |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here, until        |
|                                   | evidence is lodged or manual      |
|                                   | review comes due.                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Evidence provided or manual       |
|                                   | review falls due + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Did the customer provide all      |
|                                   | required evidence within the      |
|                                   | timeframe requested?              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, if the evidence means the    |
|                                   | customer:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   meets the eligibility         |
|                                   |     criteria                      |
|                                   |     - annotate the AGDRP/NZDRP    |
|                                   |     Claim- Grant Summary Note by  |
|                                   |     selecting the Annotate        |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   |     - record the reason why the   |
|                                   |     claim was correctly granted   |
|                                   |     - select Save                 |
|                                   |     - procedure ends here         |
|                                   | -   does not meet the eligibility |
|                                   |     criteria, this means the      |
|                                   |     customer should not have been |
|                                   |     paid. See Table 10            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, this means the customer       |
|                                   | should not have been paid. See    |
|                                   | Table 10                          |
