AGDRP or NZ DRP was incorrectly paid

Table 10: Process to follow when a customer has been incorrectly paid or
customer was not eligible for payment. This includes if an incorrect
carer was paid.

If a payment has been issued incorrectly and the payment was made by NPP
or immediate payment this cannot be stopped by the Stop Payment process
with help from the ICT Service Desk. Do not follow steps in Payment of
arrears after reassessment.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | If AGDRP or NZ DRP should not     |
|                                   | have been granted + Read more ... |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This includes where AGDRP or NZ   |
|                                   | DRP may have been paid to an      |
|                                   | incorrect carer.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the customer’s record to   |
|                                   | make sure the customer should not |
|                                   | have been paid. See Eligibility   |
|                                   | for AGDRP and NZ DRP.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Should the customer have been     |
|                                   | paid AGDRP or NZ DRP?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, payment was correctly        |
|                                   | granted:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Annotate the AGDRP/NZDRP      |
|                                   |     Claim- Grant Summary Note by  |
|                                   |     selecting the Annotate        |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Record the reason why the     |
|                                   |     claim was correctly granted   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Update the AGDRP/NZDRP Claim- |
|                                   |     Grant Summary Note with       |
|                                   |     explanation of why the claim  |
|                                   |     should not have been granted  |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 2                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Customer should not have been     |
|                                   | paid + Read more ...              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has been paid     |
|                                   | incorrectly:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Customer First              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Note: staff should not have   |
|                                   |     the customer’s record open in |
|                                   |     Customer First and Process    |
|                                   |     Direct at the same time, as   |
|                                   |     this can cause errors         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Create a minimum standards ACTDOC |
|                                   | that uses debt information using  |
|                                   | the Callback/ACTDOC guided        |
|                                   | procedure                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To find the Callback/ACTDOC   |
|                                   |     guided procedure, key         |
|                                   |     Callback/ACTDOC in the free   |
|                                   |     text field under Search       |
|                                   |     Workspace                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Service Reason         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   AUS Gov Disaster Recovery for |
|                                   |     AGDRP                         |
|                                   | -   Emergency Exgratia for NZ DRP |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Type ACTDOC                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Under Category select Debt        |
|                                   | Raising                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Generate Document Content  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Document Content, add:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Disaster event claimed        |
|                                   | -   Raise a debt for: $(enter     |
|                                   |     amount)                       |
|                                   | -   The reason the customer was   |
|                                   |     overpaid. Include the details |
|                                   |     of how the overpayment        |
|                                   |     occurred. For example:        |
|                                   |     customer not in an approved   |
|                                   |     LGA, customer is the          |
|                                   |     incorrect carer of a          |
|                                   |     child/ren (include the name   |
|                                   |     and CRN of any children       |
|                                   |     incorrectly paid)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Finish at the top left     |
|                                   | corner of the screen              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key AL in the Next field, then    |
|                                   | press [Enter] to go to the        |
|                                   | Activity List (AL) screen         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the ACTDOC activity        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select ‘O’ Transfer the activity  |
|                                   | to another site or region         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Regional Office key: XWA       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In New Keywords add keyword:      |
|                                   | DRPDET                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select OK to Are you sure you     |
|                                   | want to update the activity?      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Return to the AL screen to make   |
|                                   | sure the correct code shows under |
|                                   | Region                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff do not need to take any     |
|                                   | further action to have the ACTDOC |
|                                   | actioned. If a customer is on the |
|                                   | phone, tell them they may be      |
|                                   | contacted at a later date to      |
|                                   | discuss this further.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Contact Technical Peer Support,   |
|                                   | who will complete a payment query |
|                                   | template for escalation to the    |
|                                   | Level 2 Helpdesk, where a         |
|                                   | customer                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   received AGDRP or NZ DRP for  |
|                                   |     the New South Wales Floods –  |
|                                   |     February 2022                 |
|                                   | -   was not eligible to receive   |
|                                   |     this payment (this includes   |
|                                   |     claims identified as          |
|                                   |     fraudulent), and              |
|                                   | -   resides in a local government |
|                                   |     area eligible for the AGDRP   |
|                                   |     (Special Supplement)          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This is to make sure these        |
|                                   | customers do not incorrectly      |
|                                   | receive the AGDRP (Special        |
|                                   | Supplement).                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an incorrect carer has been    |
|                                   | paid, go to Step 3.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Otherwise, procedure ends here    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Has the correct carer lodged a    |
|                                   | claim? + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   finalise the claim on the     |
|                                   |     correct carer’s record        |
|                                   | -   grant AGDRP/NZ DRP for the    |
|                                   |     required child/ren            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, procedure ends here           |

Deceased or missing family member claims

Table 11: Process to follow for Service Officers allocated claims where
customers have indicated an immediate family member has died or missing.
This is a triage process managed by specialist staff to determine if:

the customer may genuinely meet the criteria, and

a social worker referral is appropriate

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Customer selected immediate       |
|                                   | family member deceased or missing |
|                                   | in claim                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Online claim or Assisted Customer |
|                                   | Claim (ACC) + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When a customer indicates in      |
|                                   | their online claim or ACC that an |
|                                   | immediate family member is        |
|                                   | deceased or missing, the system   |
|                                   | automatically places the keyword  |
|                                   | DTH on the claim. These claims    |
|                                   | are to be reviewed by specialised |
|                                   | staff. If determined appropriate, |
|                                   | a manual referral for Social      |
|                                   | Worker contact is created.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These manual referrals allow      |
|                                   | social workers to help:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   particularly vulnerable       |
|                                   |     customers, and                |
|                                   | -   in obtaining evidence to      |
|                                   |     confirm an immediate family   |
|                                   |     member is deceased or         |
|                                   |     missing, if the relevant      |
|                                   |     criteria are met              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 2.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Paper claims + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers are to manually  |
|                                   | create the social worker referral |
|                                   | after reviewing the claim         |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These referrals allow social      |
|                                   | workers to help:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   particularly vulnerable       |
|                                   |     customers, and                |
|                                   | -   in obtaining evidence to      |
|                                   |     confirm an immediate family   |
|                                   |     member is deceased or         |
|                                   |     missing, if the relevant      |
|                                   |     criteria are met              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 2.                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Review of claim prior to Social   |
|                                   | Worker referral if required +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers are to review    |
|                                   | the claim and determine if a      |
|                                   | Social Worker referral is         |
|                                   | appropriate.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer indicated an     |
|                                   | impact reason other than deceased |
|                                   | or missing family member?         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, assess the claim to          |
|                                   | determine if the customer is      |
|                                   | eligible under another adverse    |
|                                   | impact reason:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Customer is eligible -        |
|                                   |     process the claim to issue    |
|                                   |     the payment (go to Step 20 in |
|                                   |     Table 2 to continue           |
|                                   |     processing the claim). Then   |
|                                   |     go to Step 3                  |
|                                   | -   Customer is not eligible, go  |
|                                   |     to Step 3                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 3                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Contact customer + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make 2 genuine attempts to        |
|                                   | contact the customer.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS only) between 8:00 am and    |
|                                   | 8:00 pm using the customer's      |
|                                   | local time, to let them know a    |
|                                   | Service Officer will call them    |
|                                   | today from a private number.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer needs an      |
|                                   | interpreter, the 4 digit office   |
|                                   | code ID is 1897 for Smart Centre  |
|                                   | Emergency Management. See         |
|                                   | Contacting an on-demand telephone |
|                                   | interpreter (Interpreter          |
|                                   | Connect).                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Contact successful + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ask the customer to give Proof of |
|                                   | Record Ownership (PoRO). Do not   |
|                                   | give hints or prompts that help   |
|                                   | the customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   | questions                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If payment has been granted under |
|                                   | another adverse impact reason:    |
|                                   | Tell the customer under which     |
|                                   | impact reason their payment was   |
|                                   | granted. Offer the customer a     |
|                                   | referral to a social worker for   |
|                                   | personal support                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If offer accepted, go to Step |
|                                   |     5                             |
|                                   | -   If offer declined:            |
|                                   |     - Annotate the Claim          |
|                                   |     Finalisation Note stating the |
|                                   |     customer does not require a   |
|                                   |     social worker referral        |
|                                   |     - Procedure ends here         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If payment has not been granted   |
|                                   | under another adverse impact      |
|                                   | reason, ask more clarifying       |
|                                   | questions to determine if the     |
|                                   | customer may be eligible under    |
|                                   | another adverse impact reason     |
|                                   | (noting this may require them to  |
|                                   | live in a declared disaster       |
|                                   | area).                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If eligible and claim can be  |
|                                   |     granted, finalise the claim.  |
|                                   |     Ask the customer if they      |
|                                   |     would still like to speak to  |
|                                   |     a social worker               |
|                                   |     - If yes, go to Step 5        |
|                                   |     - If no, annotate the Claim   |
|                                   |     Finalisation Note stating the |
|                                   |     customer does not require a   |
|                                   |     social worker referral.       |
|                                   |     Procedure ends here.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If not eligible under another     |
|                                   | adverse impact reason and the     |
|                                   | customer would still like their   |
|                                   | claim to be assessed under the    |
|                                   | adverse impact reason of          |
|                                   | immediate family member is        |
|                                   | deceased or missing, go to Step 4 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Contact unsuccessful + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the Progress of Claim    |
|                                   | Note on the DL screen under the   |
|                                   | Document list/note section with   |
|                                   | the attempts made to contact the  |
|                                   | customer.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Where the customer has already    |
|                                   | been granted under another        |
|                                   | adverse impact reason, include in |
|                                   | the annotation ‘Customer granted  |
|                                   | under another adverse impact      |
|                                   | reason. Unable to contact to      |
|                                   | determine if social worker        |
|                                   | referral still required’.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select Close document         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | An immediate family member is     |
|                                   | missing or deceased + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, see eligibility         |
|                                   | criteria.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Obtain as much information as     |
|                                   | possible about the circumstances  |
|                                   | of the customer’s missing or      |
|                                   | deceased family member:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Is the deceased or missing    |
|                                   |     person an Australian          |
|                                   |     resident?                     |
|                                   | -   Is the customer an immediate  |
|                                   |     family member as per the      |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria?         |
|                                   | -   Was the deceased or missing   |
|                                   |     person in a declared area at  |
|                                   |     the time of the disaster?     |
|                                   | -   Did the person go missing or  |
|                                   |     die as a direct result of the |
|                                   |     disaster?                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If it is clear the customer will  |
|                                   | not meet this impact criteria:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Explain they will not be eligible |
|                                   | for payment and the reason why.   |
|                                   | If approval has:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   been given to reject claims,  |
|                                   |     process the claim, go to Step |
|                                   |     23 in Table 2                 |
|                                   | -   not been given, remove the    |
|                                   |     DTH keyword, go to Step 2 in  |
|                                   |     Table 3 to place the claim on |
|                                   |     hold                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ask if they would still like to   |
|                                   | speak to a social worker:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If yes, go to Step 5          |
|                                   | -   If no,                        |
|                                   |     - Annotate the Finalisation   |
|                                   |     Note stating the customer did |
|                                   |     not meet the criteria for -   |
|                                   |     deceased/missing family       |
|                                   |     member and did not want to    |
|                                   |     speak to a social worker      |
|                                   |     - Procedure ends here         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer may be eligible   |
|                                   | under this impact criteria:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Tell the customer evidence is |
|                                   |     needed to support the claim,  |
|                                   |     which may also include        |
|                                   |     evidence of their             |
|                                   |     relationship to the deceased  |
|                                   |     or missing person. See        |
|                                   |     Eligibility for AGDRP and NZ  |
|                                   |     DRP                           |
|                                   | -   If they are unable to provide |
|                                   |     evidence about the family     |
|                                   |     member, social workers can    |
|                                   |     help in confirming this       |
|                                   |     information                   |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 5                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Social worker referral + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Always offer to complete an       |
|                                   | announced (warm) transfer to the  |
|                                   | Social Work Disaster Line while   |
|                                   | customer is on the phone, if      |
|                                   | they:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   have been granted under       |
|                                   |     another adverse impact but    |
|                                   |     would still like to speak to  |
|                                   |     a social worker               |
|                                   | -   would not be eligible under   |
|                                   |     the deceased/missing family   |
|                                   |     member criteria but would     |
|                                   |     still like to speak to a      |
|                                   |     social worker, or             |
|                                   | -   may be eligible under the     |
|                                   |     deceased/missing family       |
|                                   |     member criteria               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Successful transfer               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For claims where the customer may |
|                                   | be eligible under the             |
|                                   | deceased/missing family member    |
|                                   | criteria, manually create a       |
|                                   | social worker referral by         |
|                                   | selecting:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   [more options] then Referral  |
|                                   | -   Referral Type Social Worker   |
|                                   |     Referral and Referral Reason  |
|                                   |     Disaster Event                |
|                                   | -   place the claim on hold for 7 |
|                                   |     days to allow for a social    |
|                                   |     worker assessment to be made  |
|                                   | -   Once the social worker        |
|                                   |     assessment has been           |
|                                   |     completed, they will change   |
|                                   |     the status to In Process so   |
|                                   |     it can be reallocated for     |
|                                   |     processing                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here until the |
|                                   |     social worker assessment has  |
|                                   |     been completed                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For claims where the customer’s   |
|                                   | claim has already been granted or |
|                                   | rejected, no more action is       |
|                                   | needed. Procedure ends here       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Unsuccessful transfer             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A transfer to the Social Work     |
|                                   | Disaster Line may not be possible |
|                                   | if the contact with the customer  |
|                                   | is outside of operating hours or  |
|                                   | the customer is unable to wait.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the customer’s telephone  |
|                                   | details are correct and tell the  |
|                                   | customer a social worker will     |
|                                   | contact them in due course, and   |
|                                   | they will receive a message       |
|                                   | letting them know to expect a     |
|                                   | call from a private number        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For customers who may be eligible |
|                                   | under the deceased/missing family |
|                                   | member criteria                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Annotate the Progress of      |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document list/note  |
|                                   |     section with any additional   |
|                                   |     information provided by the   |
|                                   |     customer during the           |
|                                   |     conversation                  |
|                                   |     - Select Save                 |
|                                   |     - Select Close document       |
|                                   | -   manually create a social      |
|                                   |     worker referral by selecting: |
|                                   |     - [more options] then         |
|                                   |     Referral                      |
|                                   |     - Referral Type Social Worker |
|                                   |     Referral and Referral Reason  |
|                                   |     Disaster Event                |
|                                   | -   Place the claim on hold for 7 |
|                                   |     days to allow time for the    |
|                                   |     social worker to contact the  |
|                                   |     customer and make an          |
|                                   |     assessment. The social worker |
|                                   |     will change the status to In  |
|                                   |     Process so it can be          |
|                                   |     reallocated for processing.   |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here until the |
|                                   |     social worker assessment has  |
|                                   |     been completed                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For claims where the customer’s   |
|                                   | claim has already been granted or |
|                                   | rejected, and therefore no claim  |
|                                   | processing is needed, a general   |
|                                   | disaster referral is to be        |
|                                   | created if the customer has       |
|                                   | requested personal support.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a transfer is not possible     |
|                                   | (for example, outside of          |
|                                   | operating hours or the customer   |
|                                   | is unable to wait), create a      |
|                                   | referral to a social worker using |
|                                   | the Contingency SW Disaster       |
|                                   | Referral Fast Note:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Search Workspace: Key Fast     |
|                                   | Note then select Search           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Fast Note hyperlink    |
|                                   | and complete the Fast Note        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Who contacted: From the drop down |
|                                   | box select: Customer              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Reason: From the drop     |
|                                   | down box select the following:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   AGDRP select AGP - AUS Gov    |
|                                   |     Disaster Recovery Payment     |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP select EXG - Emergency |
|                                   |     Ex-gratia                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date of Receipt: Date DOC created |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Channel: From the drop down box   |
|                                   | select:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   phone claims lodged using     |
|                                   |     Assisted Customer Claim,      |
|                                   |     select PHO                    |
|                                   | -   online claims select WEB      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Source: From the drop down        |
|                                   | select:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   phone claims lodged using     |
|                                   |     Assisted Customer Claim,      |
|                                   |     select PHO                    |
|                                   | -   online claims select OLC      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Auto text. From the drop   |
|                                   | down box select:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Category 1: Social Worker     |
|                                   | -   Category 2: Claims            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Template: Contingency SW Disaster |
|                                   | Referral                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Confirm                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete Brief details of         |
|                                   | Referral reason                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check if there is an existing     |
|                                   | social work referral on the       |
|                                   | Activity tab in Customer First or |
|                                   | on the Work List in Process       |
|                                   | Direct. If there is a referral    |
|                                   | pending:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update additional notes in the    |
|                                   | original referral. Do not create  |
|                                   | a new referral                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Tell the customer:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ‘a social worker will call    |
|                                   |     you as soon as possible’      |
|                                   | -   ‘a social worker will send    |
|                                   |     you a text before they call’  |
|                                   |     (if the customer is           |
|                                   |     registered for pre call SMS). |
|                                   |     ‘The call will come from a    |
|                                   |     private number’               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the customer’s correct      |
|                                   | contact details are recorded      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Create a DOC on the customer’s    |
|                                   | record to note the contact        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
